(1) The municipal office of a municipality with extended powers shall provide the regional authority with assistance and the data necessary for the preparation and updating of the drought plan for the region and for the activities of the regional drought commission.

(2) At the request of a drought authority, everyone is obliged to provide it with known information that may influence the issuance of measures during a state of water scarcity. This does not affect the duty of confidentiality imposed or recognized by another legal regulation.

§ 87m

The regional authority shall prepare a report on the course of the state of water scarcity within 6 months from the day of the revocation of the state of water scarcity. It shall send the report to the Ministry of Agriculture and the Ministry of the Environment. The central drought commission shall inform the government about the course and consequences of the state of water scarcity.

TITLE XI
FEES

Division 1
Fee for the Quantity of Abstracted Groundwater

Section 1
The Fee

§ 88
Payer of the Fee

(1) The payer of the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is the person authorized by a permit for the abstraction of groundwater.

(2) In the event that the person authorized under paragraph 1 has enabled the exercise of their permit for the management of waters under § 11 para. 3 to the operator of a water supply system for public use under the act regulating water supply and sewerage systems, the payer of the fee is this operator of the water supply system for public use.

§ 88a
Subject Matter of the Fee

The subject matter of the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is the abstraction of groundwater under § 8 para. 1 let. b) point 1.

§ 88b
Exemption from the Fee

The abstraction of groundwater carried out by the fee payer in the territory of a single municipality or military district is exempt from the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater, provided its volume does not exceed 6,000 m³ in a calendar year or does not exceed 500 m³ in any month of the calendar year.

§ 88c
Fee Base

The base for the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is the volume of abstracted water in m³.

§ 88d
Fee Rate

The rate for the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is provided in Annex No. 2 to this Act.

§ 88e
Calculation of the Fee

The fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is calculated as the product of the fee base and the fee rate.

§ 88f
Fee Period

The fee period for the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is the calendar year.

§ 88g
Budgetary Allocation of the Fee

The revenue from the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is
a) 50% revenue for the budget of the region in whose territory the groundwater abstraction takes place, and
b) 50% revenue for the budget of the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic.

§ 88h
Earmarking of the Fee

(1) The portion of the revenue from the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater that is revenue for the budget of the region may be used only to support the construction and renewal of water management infrastructure, specifically for the municipality in whose territory the groundwater abstraction takes place, and for the establishment and replenishment of the special account under § 42 para. 4.

(2) The portion of the revenue from the fee that is revenue for the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic may be used for improving the protection of water quality and quantity and for monitoring water quantity and quality.

Section 2
Administration of the Fee

§ 88i
Fee Administrator

(1) The administrator of the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic.

(2) The administration of the payment of the fee is carried out by the customs office. The local competence of the customs office is determined by the registered office or place of residence of the fee payer.

§ 88j
Fee Declaration

(1) The payer of the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is obliged to file a fee declaration no later than February 15 of the calendar year following the end of the fee period.

(2) The fee declaration is submitted through the integrated system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment.

(3) A fee declaration is not submitted if the abstraction of groundwater is exempt from the fee.

(4) The template for the fee declaration and the supplementary fee declaration is issued by the fee administrator.

§ 88k
Fee Due Date

The fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater is due within 30 days from the date the payment assessment becomes final.

§ 88l
Interest on Late Payment

In the case of a shortfall on the fee for the quantity of abstracted groundwater, interest on late payment shall arise.

Division 2
Fee for the Discharge of Wastewater into Surface Waters

Section 1
The Fee

§ 89
Payer of the Fee

The payer of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is the person who discharges wastewater into surface waters.

§ 89a
Subject Matter of the Fee

(1) The subject matter of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is the discharge of wastewater from an individual source of pollution into surface waters.

(2) A source of pollution is understood as the territory of a municipality, the territory of a military district, an industrial area, a building, or a facility, if wastewater is discharged from them separately into surface waters.

§ 89b
Exemption from the Fee

The following are exempt from the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters:
a) the discharge of mineral waters abstracted from a source certified under the act regulating spa services as a natural medicinal source, if they were not used in spa care,
b) the discharge of natural mineral waters abstracted from a source certified under the act regulating spa services as a source of natural mineral water, if they were not used in the production of bottled mineral water,
c) the discharge of water from remediation wells and systems,
d) the discharge of wastewater from the once-through cooling of steam turbines,
e) the discharge of wastewater resulting from the use of groundwater or surface water for obtaining thermal energy under § 8 para. 1 let. d), or
f) the discharge of wastewater from the relief chambers of a unified sewer system⁶⁴) that meets the technical requirements for their construction and operation as stipulated by the legal regulation implementing the Act on Water Supply and Sewerage Systems.

§ 89c
Exemption from Partial Fees

(1) The discharge of wastewater whose volume does not exceed 100,000 m³ during the fee period is exempt from the partial fee based on volume.

(2) The discharge of wastewater that does not exceed the mass or concentration limit for the indicator of that pollution specified in Annex No. 2 to this Act is exempt from the partial fee for individual pollution.

§ 89d
Fee Base

The base for the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters consists of partial fee bases.

§ 89e
Partial Fee Bases

(1) The partial fee bases are
a) the volume of wastewater in m³ in the case of the partial fee based on volume, and
b) the total quantity of individual pollution specified in Annex No. 2 to this Act contained in the wastewater, in kg, in the case of the partial fee for that pollution.

(2) The fee payer may reduce the partial fee base for individual pollution by the total quantity of that pollution contained in the abstracted water from which the discharged wastewater originated.

(3) For the purpose of calculating the fee, the total quantity of individual pollution in the water in kg is calculated as the product of
a) the average concentration of the indicator of that pollution specified in Annex No. 2 to this Act in the water in kg/m ³, and
b) the volume of water in m³.

(4) If the operation of a wastewater treatment plant is limited or interrupted as a result of a flood or other natural disaster, the total quantity of individual pollution in the water under paragraph 3 for the period when the operation was limited or interrupted is considered to be the product of
a) the number of days the operation was limited or interrupted, and
b) the ratio of the total quantity of individual pollution in the water for the preceding fee period to the number of days of that fee period.

§ 89f
Fee Rate

(1) The rate for the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is provided in Annex No. 2 to this Act.

(2) When calculating the fee for organic pollution of discharged wastewater, a different rate is used for treated and untreated wastewater.

(3) For the purposes of calculating the fee, treated wastewater is considered to be water that meets the values of the emission standards set in the government regulation under § 38 para. 10; if no emission standard is set, the emission limits for the discharge of wastewater specified in the permit under § 8 para. 1 let. c) apply.

§ 89g
Reduction of the Partial Fee

(1) If, for an individual pollutant, a reduction in its discharged quantity is achieved as a result of the implementation of a technical or technological measure with a permanent effect compared to the immediately preceding fee period, a reduction on the partial fee may be claimed.

(2) The reduction on the partial fee for an individual pollutant is the product of
a) the partial fee base,
b) the rate for this partial fee base,
c) the ratio of

the difference between the partial fee base in the immediately preceding fee period and the partial fee base, and

the partial fee base in the immediately preceding fee period, and
d) a coefficient of 2.5.

(3) The reduction under paragraph 2 shall not exceed the product of the partial fee base and the rate for this partial fee base.

(4) A reduction cannot be claimed if the ratio under paragraph 2 let. c) is lower than 0.1.

§ 89h
Calculation of the Fee

The fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is calculated as the sum of the partial fee based on volume and the partial fees for individual pollutants.

§ 89i
Calculation of Partial Fees

The partial fee is calculated as the difference between
a) the product of the partial fee base and the rate for this partial fee base, and
b) the reduction on the partial fee claimed by the fee payer.

§ 89j
Fee Period

The fee period for the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is the calendar year.

§ 89k
Budgetary Allocation of the Fee

The revenue from the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is revenue for the budget of the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic.

§ 89l
Earmarking of the Fee

The revenue from the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters may be used to support the intensification and construction of water management infrastructure and to cover the costs of the activities of the accredited laboratory selected by the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic (hereinafter "control laboratory") and of professionally competent persons authorized to conduct business and authorized to perform official flow measurements with open-channel meters under the Metrology Act.

Section 2
Administration of the Fee

§ 89m
Fee Administrator

(1) The administrator of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic.

(2) The administration of the payment of the fee is carried out by the customs office. The local competence of the customs office is determined by the registered office or place of residence of the fee payer.

§ 89n
Obligations of the Fee Payer

(1) The payer of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is obliged to keep operational records on the monitoring of the quantity of discharged pollution, the volume of discharged wastewater, and other facts relevant for determining the amount of the fee. The fee payer is obliged to retain all documents for keeping the operational records for a period of 5 years.

(2) The fee payer is obliged, for each source and outfall, through an accredited laboratory, to take samples of wastewater and monitor the concentration of pollution in them for the relevant indicators according to Annex No. 2, part B, to determine the average concentration of individual pollutants, and to measure the volume of wastewater discharged from the source of pollution. The fee payer is responsible for the correctness of determining the sources of pollution and establishing the concentration of pollution according to the relevant pollution indicators.

(3) The fee payer is obliged to notify the fee administrator without undue delay of any limitation, interruption, and resumption of the operation of the wastewater treatment plant.

(4) If the fee payer reduces the partial fee base for an individual pollutant by the total quantity of this pollution contained in the abstracted water from which the discharged wastewater originated, they are obliged to ascertain the quantity of this pollution.

(5) The Ministry of the Environment shall, by decree, determine
a) the particulars of the operational records under paragraph 1,
b) a more detailed definition of the source of pollution under § 89a para. 1,
c) the procedure for determining the pollution contained in wastewater, including the measurement methods for pollution indicators by the accredited and control laboratory,
d) the method of determining the average concentration of individual pollutants and the method of measuring the volume of wastewater discharged from the source of pollution under paragraph 2,
e) the method of determining the quantity of pollution in the abstracted water from which the discharged wastewater originated under paragraph 4.

§ 89o
Fee Declaration

(1) The payer of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is obliged to file a fee declaration no later than February 15 of the calendar year following the end of the fee period.

(2) The fee declaration is submitted through the integrated system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment.

(3) A fee declaration is not submitted if the discharge of wastewater is fully exempt from the fee.

(4) The template for the fee declaration and the supplementary fee declaration is issued by the fee administrator.

§ 89p
Fee Due Date

The fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is due within 30 days from the date the payment assessment becomes final.

§ 89q
Interest on Late Payment

In the case of a shortfall on the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters, interest on late payment shall arise.

Division 3
Fee for the Permitted Discharge of Wastewater into Groundwaters

Section 1
The Fee

§ 90
Payer of the Fee

The payer of the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is the person authorized who has a permit for the discharge of wastewater into groundwaters.

§ 90a
Subject Matter of the Fee

The subject matter of the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is the discharge of wastewater into groundwaters on the basis of a permit from a facility intended for the treatment of wastewater.

§ 90b
Exemption from the Fee

The following are exempt from the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters:
a) the discharge of wastewater from a facility intended for the treatment of wastewater from one residential building or one building for family recreation,
b) the discharge of mineral waters abstracted from a source certified under the act regulating spa services as a natural medicinal source, if they were not used in spa care,
c) the discharge of natural mineral waters abstracted from a source certified under the act regulating spa services as a source of natural mineral water, if they were not used in the production of bottled mineral water,
d) the discharge of wastewater resulting from the use of groundwater or surface water for obtaining thermal energy [§ 8 para. 1 let. d)], and
e) the discharge of contaminated waters, the contamination of which was reduced after their extraction from groundwaters [§ 8 para. 1 let. e)].

§ 90c
Fee Base

The base for the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is the capacity of the facility intended for the treatment of wastewater from which the wastewater is discharged, expressed in population equivalents. One population equivalent corresponds to a pollution production of 60 g BOD₅ per day.

§ 90d
Fee Rate

The rate for the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is CZK 350.

§ 90e
Calculation of the Fee

The fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is calculated as the product of the fee base rounded up to the nearest whole population equivalent and the fee rate.

§ 90f
Fee Period

The fee period for the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is the calendar year.

§ 90g
Budgetary Allocation of the Fee

The revenue from the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is revenue for the budget of the municipality in whose territory the discharge occurs.

Section 2
Administration of the Fee

§ 90h
Fee Administrator

The administrator of the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is the municipal office of the municipality in whose territory the discharge occurs.

§ 90i
Fee Due Date

The fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters is due by January 31 of the calendar year following the fee period.

Division 1
repealed

§ 91 – § 100
repealed

TITLE XII
Payment for the Administration of Watercourses and River Basins and Reimbursement of Expenditures on Measures in the Public Interest

§ 101
Payment for the Administration of Watercourses and River Basins

(1) Whoever abstracts surface water from a watercourse is obliged to pay a payment for the administration of watercourses and, in the case of abstractions of surface water from significant watercourses and from other surface waters, also for the administration of the river basin, according to the purpose of use of the abstracted surface water at a unit rate in CZK/m³ according to the actually abstracted quantity of surface water. Whoever abstracts surface water is obliged, for each day of delay in paying the payments under the first sentence, to pay interest on late payment at a rate of 1 per mille. The obligation to pay this payment is also held by a person who abstracts surface water through the facility of another authorized person, who does not pay for the abstraction of surface water under paragraph 4.

(2) The amount of the payment is calculated by multiplying the quantity of surface water actually abstracted during the past calendar month (or another period not exceeding one calendar year, agreed upon with the watercourse administrator in which the surface water abstraction occurs) reduced by the quantity of surface water to which the payment does not apply (paragraph 4), by the price for the abstraction of surface water determined by the watercourse administrator under a special act.⁴²) If the person authorized to manage waters abstracts surface water from a water source at one location at multiple points, then for the purpose of charging, the abstracted quantity of surface water is summed.

(3) The price for the abstraction of surface water is determined separately for the purposes of use for
a) once-through cooling of steam turbines,
b) agricultural irrigation,
c) flooding of artificial terrain depressions (residual pits after mineral extraction) in cases requiring the pumping or transfer of water; this price may not exceed the amount of operating costs incurred by the watercourse administrator for this activity,
d) other abstractions.

(4) The payment for the abstraction of surface water is not paid if the abstracted quantity of surface water is less than or equal to 6,000 m³ in a calendar year or is less than or equal to 500 m³ in any month of the calendar year. It is also not paid for the abstraction of surface water for the operation of fish hatcheries and nurseries and for the filling of ponds and water reservoirs for fish farming, the flooding of artificial terrain depressions (residual pits after mineral extraction) not requiring the pumping or transfer of water by the watercourse administrator, for the once-through cooling of nuclear research reactors, for firefighting purposes, the filling of public swimming pools, abandoned arms of watercourses and reservoirs forming a protected biotope of plants and animals, for preserving internationally important wetlands in alluvial forests, for spraying stored timber with water, for the production of snow by snow cannons, for the abstraction of turbid water for agricultural or forestry production, for a permitted abstraction to compensate for the moisture deficit of agricultural crops, including nursery plants, and for filling water reservoirs for the accumulation of surface water for the irrigation of agricultural crops and nursery plants under the conditions of a valid permit for the management of waters. Turbid waters for agricultural and forestry production are surface waters abstracted from a watercourse during increased flows (water levels) for irrigation by flooding.

(5) The person authorized for the abstraction of surface water is obliged to pay the payment monthly by the twenty-fifth day after the end of the calendar month to the relevant watercourse administrator in which the surface water abstraction occurs; for other abstractions of surface water, to the relevant river basin administrator, unless they agree on other payment terms with them; however, a longer deadline than January 25 of the following calendar year cannot be agreed upon in this agreement.

(6) If the person who abstracted surface water fails to pay the due payment, the relevant watercourse administrator in which the surface water abstraction occurs, or the relevant river basin administrator for the place of other surface water abstraction, is entitled to claim it, including interest on late payment under paragraph 1, in court.

§ 102
Reimbursement of Expenditures on Measures in the Public Interest

(1) The state may provide financial resources to reimburse expenditures on measures in the public interest, in particular for
a) the activities of river basin administration under this Act,
b) the administration of minor watercourses,
c) the assessment and evaluation of the status of surface and groundwaters,
d) planning in the water sector,
e) studies of runoff conditions, the establishment of floodplains, and studies of preventive flood protection measures,
f) the renewal of waterworks and watercourse beds,
g) the establishment, renewal, and operation of waterworks and facilities for protection against floods and droughts,
h) increasing the capacity and modifying the beds of watercourses and improving runoff conditions in the landscape,
i) the establishment and renewal of structures for water management land improvements,
j) the renewal, desilting, and reconstruction of ponds,
k) the renewal and operation of waterways,
l) the administration of waterworks for which no one cares and for which no owner is known,
m) other measures under the approved programs of measures (§ 26),
n) the renewal of a watercourse bed after a flood (§ 45 para. 1),
o) carrying out control assessments of the quality and quantity of discharged wastewater, including the identification of sources of pollution,
p) the infiltration, retention, and drainage of stormwater,
q) economic entities engaged in agricultural primary production in the protection zones of water resources and the protection zones of water supply reservoirs.

(2) The state provides financial resources for measures in the public interest to river basin administrators, the Czech Environmental Inspectorate, watercourse administrators, owners of waterworks, and authorized expert bodies (§ 21 para. 3) and other natural and legal persons; there is no legal entitlement to financial resources.

TITLE XIII
MEASUREMENT OF WASTEWATER VOLUME AND SAMPLING AND ANALYSIS OF WASTEWATER SAMPLES FOR THE PURPOSE OF DETERMINING THE FEE FOR THE DISCHARGE OF WASTEWATER INTO SURFACE WATERS

§ 103
Measurement of Wastewater Volume

(1) The correctness of the measurement of the volume of discharged wastewater and the proper function of the measuring device may only be controlled by a professionally competent person authorized to conduct business and certified for the performance of official flow measurements with open-channel meters under the Metrology Act.

(2) The correctness of the measurement of the volume of discharged wastewater for the purpose of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is controlled by a professionally competent person under paragraph 1, selected by the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic.

(3) The list of professionally competent persons under paragraph 2 shall be published by the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic in a manner enabling remote access.

(4) The eligible costs of the professionally competent persons under paragraph 2 associated with the control of the correctness of the measurement of the volume of discharged wastewater for the purpose of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters shall be paid by the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic from the revenue of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters.

(5) The person who discharges wastewater into surface waters is obliged to allow the professionally competent person under paragraph 2 to enter the premises where the source of pollution is located and to ensure the conditions for carrying out the control, including the provision of the necessary documents for the control.

§ 103a
Sampling and Analysis of Wastewater Samples for the Purpose of Determining Fees for the Discharge of Wastewater into Surface Waters

(1) The sampling and analysis of wastewater samples discharged from a source of pollution for the purpose of determining the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters shall be carried out by an accredited laboratory at the request of the person who discharges the wastewater.

(2) The correctness of the monitoring of discharged pollution in discharged wastewater for the purpose of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters is controlled by a control laboratory.

(3) The list of control laboratories shall be published by the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic in a manner enabling remote access.

(4) The eligible costs of the control laboratory associated with the performance of sampling and sample analysis shall be paid by the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic from the revenue of the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters.

(5) The person who discharges wastewater into surface waters is obliged to allow the staff of the control laboratory to enter the premises where the source of pollution is located and to ensure the conditions for sampling from all outfalls of the pollution source.

TITLE XIV
PERFORMANCE OF STATE ADMINISTRATION

§ 104

(1) State administration under this Act is performed by water authorities and the Czech Environmental Inspectorate.

(2) Water authorities are
a) municipal offices,
b) district offices⁴³) in the territory of military districts,
c) municipal offices of municipalities with extended powers,
d) regional authorities,
e) ministries as the central water authority (§ 108).
This does not affect the provisions on flood authorities and drought authorities.

(3) In administrative proceedings conducted under the Act on Nature and Landscape Protection¹⁴ᵃ⁾, the Mining Act¹ᵃ⁾, and the Act on Mining Activities, Explosives, and the State Mining Administration⁷ᵇ⁾, and also in procedures under the Building Act⁴⁾ for the location, permitting, use, and removal of structures, a decision may be issued or another action may be taken only on the basis of a binding opinion of the water authority, if interests under this Act may be affected. A binding opinion under this provision is not issued if consent under § 17 is granted. The water authority, in a binding opinion, shall assess the possibility of deteriorating the status or ecological potential of a surface water body or the status of a groundwater body or the impossibility of achieving good status or good ecological potential of a surface water body or good status of a groundwater body. If it concludes that the implementation of the project may lead to a deterioration of the status or ecological potential of a surface water body or the status of a groundwater body or prevent the achievement of good status or good ecological potential of a surface water body or good status of a groundwater body, it shall inform the applicant that without an exemption under § 23a para. 8 it is not possible to permit or carry out the project and that without this exemption, a positive binding opinion cannot be issued. The water authority is bound by its previous binding opinion. Subsequent binding opinions may be applied by water authorities in the same matter only on the basis of newly identified and documented facts that could not have been applied earlier and which substantially change the conditions under which the original binding opinion was issued, or facts arising from a more detailed documentation or basis for the decision or other act of the administrative authority in the procedures under the first sentence, otherwise they shall not be considered.

§ 105
Municipal Offices and District Offices

(1) Municipal offices shall regulate, restrict, or, where applicable, prohibit under § 6 para. 4 of this Act the general management of surface waters, unless it concerns watercourses forming state borders.

(2) State administration in the territory of military districts is performed by district offices under §§ 105 to 107, unless it concerns powers under Titles XI and XV of this Act.

§ 106
Municipal Offices of Municipalities with Extended Powers

(1) The powers that belong to water authorities shall be exercised by the municipal offices of municipalities with extended powers, unless the Act confers them on other bodies.

(2) Municipal offices of municipalities with extended powers shall apply their opinions to the land-use plans and regulatory plans, with the exception of the land-use plans of these municipalities.

§ 107
Regional Authorities

(1) The competence of regional authorities includes
a) applying opinions to the principles of territorial development and to the land-use plans of municipalities with extended powers,
b) expressing an opinion under § 18 of this Act on constructions, if they decisively influence water management, water protection, or flood protection, and if they reserve this right,
c) deciding on matters concerning transboundary waters, with the exception of measures issued during a state of water scarcity under § 87k para. 1, after consultation with the Ministry of Agriculture and the Ministry of the Environment; if such a decision affects the course, nature, or marking of the state border, it shall be decided after consultation also with the Ministry of the Interior; if such a decision concerns natural mineral waters and natural medicinal sources near the state borders under a special act,²⁾ it shall be decided after consultation also with the Ministry of Health; transboundary waters are considered to be surface, or possibly groundwater, defined in international treaties by which the Czech Republic is bound⁴⁴⁾,
d) taking measures in extraordinary situations, especially in case of water scarcity and accidents, in cases extending beyond the territory of the administrative district of a municipality with extended powers or the capabilities of the municipal office of a municipality with extended powers,
e) cooperating with the central water authorities and river basin administrators in the preparation of sub-basin plans and their implementation. Regional authorities may, for ensuring cooperation on sub-basin plans and in controlling the implementation of sub-basin plans, request the cooperation of expert bodies, bodies monitoring the quality and health safety of water, nature protection authorities, associations of citizens active in the field of environmental protection, fisheries, owners and operators of water supply and sewerage systems, and where applicable, other bodies,
f) deciding on an exemption under § 23a para. 8 and imposing measures that establish, in the public interest, programs of measures under § 26 para. 4,
g) controlling the implementation of technical safety supervision over the waterworks it permits,
h) deciding on the classification of a waterwork into categories from the perspective of technical safety supervision, if it reserves this right,
i) determining the manner and conditions for the discharge of mine waters into surface or groundwaters and of contaminated waters and leachates from disposal sites into surface waters,
j) permitting the management of waters for the utilization of energy potential under § 8 para. 1 let. a) point 3 on significant watercourses in cases where it reserves this right,
k) permitting the discharge of wastewater into surface waters from sources of pollution of a size of 10,000 population equivalents or more,
l) permitting the discharge of wastewater from the extraction and processing of uranium ores and from nuclear power plants, and wastewater containing particularly hazardous or hazardous substances according to Annex No. 1 into surface waters, and the discharge of wastewater containing a particularly hazardous substance or a priority hazardous substance into a sewer system (§ 16), with the exception of cases where a facility with sufficient efficiency under § 16 para. 5 is installed,
m) permitting the pumping of contaminated groundwaters for the purpose of reducing their contamination and their subsequent discharge into these waters, or possibly into surface waters [§ 8 para. 1 let. e)],
n) permitting the impoundment and accumulation of surface waters in reservoirs with a total volume of over 1,000,000 m³ or with an impoundment height of over 10 m from the foundation bottom,
o) determining, at the proposal of the river basin administrator, the extent of the floodplains of significant watercourses and their active zones, imposing on the river basin administrator the preparation of such a proposal, and establishing restrictive conditions in these floodplains under § 67 para. 3,
p) deciding in cases of doubt as to whether it is surface or groundwater, what type of water management it is, or whether it is wastewater,
r) deciding in cases of doubt as to whether it is a watercourse under § 43 para. 2, as well as that other surface waters than those mentioned in paragraph 1 are a watercourse,
s) issuing an opinion under § 18 in cases where it is competent to issue a permit or consent,
t) permitting exemptions for the use of harmful substances (§ 39 para. 7) and permitting the management of waters for the purpose of fish or waterfowl farming, or possibly other animals, if the water authority sets conditions in the permit for the use of harmful substances,
u) exercising the powers of a special building authority for waterworks enabling the management of waters under letters l) to n),
v) deciding in cases where it is competent to permit waterworks, also on other matters concerning these waterworks and on the protection zones of water resources related to them, and granting exemptions from the prohibition of entry into the protection zone of a water source of the I. degree in cases where it is competent to establish the protection zone,
w) approving the manipulation rules of the waterworks it permits, including extraordinary manipulations on them, and complex manipulation rules, if at least one of the waterworks to which the complex manipulation rule will apply falls within its competence,
x) exercising the powers of a special building authority for wastewater treatment plants serving for the management of waters under letter k), and if it reserves this right, also for other waterworks associated with this management,
y) requiring from the owners (administrators) of waterworks of categories I to III, who have been obliged to ensure the implementation of technical safety supervision, the preparation of data on the parameters of a possible special flood, especially the characteristics of flow waves and the extent of the threatened area, and their provision to the relevant flood authorities, crisis management authorities, and components of the integrated rescue system,
z) deciding in cases of doubt about the scope of obligations and rights under § 53.

(2) Regional authorities are the authorities concerned under § 104 para. 9 and issue a binding opinion in matters concerning their competence.

§ 108
Ministries as the Central Water Authority

(1) Unless this Act provides otherwise, the powers of the central water authority are exercised by the Ministry of Agriculture.

(2) The Ministry of Agriculture and the Ministry of the Environment apply their opinions to the spatial development policy, the spatial development plan, and the principles of territorial development.

(3) The Ministry of the Environment exercises the powers of the central water authority in matters of
a) protection of the quantity and quality of surface and groundwaters, namely

permitting the discharge of wastewater into surface or groundwaters [§ 8 para. 1 let. c)],

permitting the pumping of contaminated groundwaters for the purpose of reducing their contamination and their subsequent discharge into these waters, or possibly into surface waters [§ 8 para. 1 let. e)],

permitting the discharge of wastewater containing particularly hazardous substances or priority hazardous substances into sewer systems (§ 16),

consent under § 17 para. 1 let. e) and i),

determining the minimum residual flow and imposing the obligation to install a benchmark or water mark on a waterwork and the obligation to regularly measure the minimum residual flow and to submit reports on the measurement results to the water authority and the river basin administrator (§ 36),

determining the minimum groundwater level and imposing the obligation to submit a draft of an intake regulation, or an obligation to regularly measure the groundwater level, the method of measurement, and the obligation to submit reports on the measurement results to the water authority and the river basin administrator (§ 37),

activities in permitting the discharge of wastewater into surface or groundwaters and taking over the results of measuring the volume of discharged water and the degree of its pollution (§ 38),

preparing a draft of the implementing regulation which determines the indicators and values of permissible water pollution (§§ 31, 32, 33, 35, and 38),
b) assessing and evaluating the status of surface and groundwaters jointly with the Ministry of Agriculture (§§ 21 and 22),
c) assessing and evaluating the status of surface and groundwaters through authorized expert bodies established by it (§ 21),
d) creating and maintaining an information system jointly with the Ministry of Agriculture under this Act (§§ 19 and 22),
e) preparing and approving plans in the water sector and preparing programs of measures jointly with the Ministry of Agriculture (§§ 24 to 26),
f) assessing plans in the water sector from the perspective of their impact on the environment (§§ 24 and 25),
g) protected areas of natural water accumulation (§ 28),
h) protection of water resources (§§ 29 and 30),
i) sensitive areas (§ 32),
j) vulnerable areas, with the exception of the review of the action programme, (§ 33),
k) determining remedial measures in case of unsatisfactory quality of surface waters used for bathing (§ 34 para. 2),
l) determining surface waters that are suitable for the life and reproduction of native species of fish and other aquatic animals jointly with the Ministry of Agriculture (§ 35),
m) protecting the quality of surface or groundwaters from harmful substances (§ 39),
n) the disposal of accidents (§ 41) and the removal of their harmful consequences (§ 42),
o) flood protection (§§ 63 to 87),
p) directing the Czech Hydrometeorological Institute (§ 73),
q) managing drought and water scarcity jointly with the Ministry of Agriculture (§§ 87a to 87m),
r) fees for groundwater abstraction jointly with the Ministry of Agriculture (Title XI, Division 1),
s) fees for the discharge of wastewater into surface and groundwaters (Title XI, Divisions 2 and 3),
t) cooperation with regional authorities in their delegated capacity in matters of protecting the quantity and quality of transboundary waters (§ 107),
u) directing the Czech Environmental Inspectorate (§ 112),
v) directing basic and applied research in the field of protecting water quantity and quality,
w) fulfilling tasks arising from the relationship with the European Communities in the field of water protection, submitting reports on the implementation of the relevant directives of the European Communities, and coordinating the transposition and implementation of the legislation of the European Communities in the field of water jointly with the Ministry of Agriculture,
x) ensuring the coordination of plans in the water sector and programs of measures within the framework of international cooperation on water protection in the river basin districts of the Elbe, Danube, and Oder.

(4) The Ministry of Transport exercises the powers of the central water authority in matters of the use of surface waters for navigation (§ 7).

(5) The Ministry of Defence exercises the powers of the central water authority in matters where the powers of the district offices under § 105 para. 2 are established.

(6) The Ministry of Agriculture and the Ministry of the Environment are the authorities concerned in assessing the maturity of projects of common interest in energy infrastructure and apply a binding opinion in a joint land-use and building proceeding for the construction of projects of common interest in energy infrastructure⁵⁵) from the perspective of the powers of all water authorities, with the exception of the powers under paragraphs 4 and 5.

§ 109
Powers of the Water Authority in Extraordinary Measures

(1) If required by the public interest, especially in case of a temporary water shortage or if the supply of water to the population is threatened or in the event of a one-time abstraction of drinking water from a water supply network in cases of rescue work during extraordinary events, fires, and other natural disasters, an intervention by the Fire Rescue Service of the Czech Republic and fire protection units, or the armed forces of the Czech Republic, the water authority may, by a decision or a measure of a general nature, without compensation, regulate for a strictly necessary period, or possibly restrict or even prohibit, permitted water management. These measures shall be taken after consultation with the affected subjects, unless the extraordinariness of the situation precludes it.

(2) If, as a result of an extraordinary situation, the permitted abstractions of surface or groundwater are restricted or prevented, leading to a serious threat to the public interest, the water authority is obliged to ensure, after consultation with the relevant authorities, remedial measures. In doing so, it may determine who, in what manner, and to what extent is obliged to carry out measures to ensure a substitute abstraction of water, or its transport. The necessary costs associated with the imposed measures may be claimed by the water authority from the person who caused the extraordinary restriction or prevention of abstractions. General regulations on liability for damages are not affected by this.

§ 110
Water Management Supervision by Water Authorities

(1) Water authorities shall control compliance with the provisions of the Water Act and the regulations issued thereunder and, within the scope of their powers, shall impose measures to remedy identified defects.

(2) Water authorities are obliged, within the scope of their powers, to control whether the decisions and measures of a general nature issued by them are being complied with.

(3) Municipal offices of municipalities with extended powers shall control compliance with the measures of a general nature issued by the drought commissions. Regional authorities shall control compliance with the decisions issued by the regional drought commission. The Ministry of Agriculture and the Ministry of the Environment shall control compliance with the decisions issued by the central drought commission.

(4) Water authorities may, when carrying out water management supervision, request the cooperation of expert bodies, bodies monitoring the quality and health safety of water, nature protection authorities, associations of citizens active in the field of environmental protection, fisheries, and where applicable, other bodies.

(5) Municipal offices of municipalities with extended powers and regional authorities, as part of water management supervision, shall supervise waterworks whose condition could endanger the safety of persons or property. In particular, they shall control how the owners or users of these structures ensure technical safety supervision and how they carry out the necessary measures for their safety.

§ 111
Higher Water Management Supervision

(1) The Ministry of Agriculture and the Ministry of the Environment shall, within the framework of higher water management supervision, control how the water authorities and the Czech Environmental Inspectorate implement the provisions of the Water Act and the regulations issued thereunder.

(2) The Ministry of Agriculture and the Ministry of the Environment are, within the scope of their powers under this Act, also authorized, within the framework of higher water management supervision, to control how the provisions of the Water Act and the regulations issued thereunder are complied with, how the decisions of water authorities are complied with, how the obligations of the owners of waterworks, watercourse administrators, and river basin administrators are fulfilled. If they identify defects, they may impose the necessary measures for their remedy.

(3) The Ministry of Agriculture, in conjunction with the Ministry of the Environment, shall submit to the government annually a report on the evaluation of the control activities carried out in the past year within the framework of higher water management supervision.

§ 112
Czech Environmental Inspectorate

(1) The Czech Environmental Inspectorate is responsible for
a) controlling, within the framework of water management supervision, how natural persons conducting business or legal persons comply with the obligations established by this Act or imposed under this Act by it or by water authorities in the area of

managing surface or groundwaters,

protecting said waters, including their protection during navigation,

accidents threatening the quality of these waters,

waterworks intended for the treatment of pollution in wastewater or for its discharge into surface or groundwaters or into sewer systems,

protecting water conditions and water resources,

bringing the discharge of wastewater into surface or groundwaters into compliance with the requirements of the Act in cases requiring special attention,
b) ordering the removal and remedy of identified defects, their causes, and harmful consequences, if it finds a violation of obligations in the areas listed under letter a),
c) ordering, in the area where it is competent to carry out control, the cessation of production or other activity if it seriously endangers the public interest and the environment, until the defects, or their causes, are remedied,
d) cooperating with the water authorities and the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic,
e) keeping a central record of accidents under § 40 et seq.,
f) controlling the compliance of polluters with the provisions on fees for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters,
g) carrying out control assessments of the quality and quantity of discharged wastewater, including the identification of sources of pollution,
h) deciding in cases of doubt as to whether it is treated wastewater for the purpose of calculating the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters,
i) fulfilling other tasks under this Act.

(2) The provisions of § 115 apply to proceedings conducted by the Czech Environmental Inspectorate under this Act, if the nature of these proceedings so permits.

§ 113
repealed

§ 114
Performance of Water Management Supervision

(1) Authorized employees of water authorities and the Czech Environmental Inspectorate shall, when performing water management supervision under this Act, present an identity card issued by the relevant control authority, which is a document of their authorization for control.

(2) No compensation is due to the person from whom a sample was taken for the purposes of water management supervision under this Act.

§ 114a
repealed

§ 115
Water Management Proceedings

(1) Unless this Act provides otherwise, water authorities shall proceed in proceedings on matters regulated by the Water Act according to the Building Act,⁴⁾ if it concerns decision-making related to waterworks and water management modifications.

(2) The Ministry of Agriculture, in cooperation with the Ministry of the Environment, shall by decree determine in which cases and which documents must be submitted with an application for a decision, a binding opinion issued within a joint land-use and building proceeding⁴⁾, a final use permit, the establishment of a protection zone of a waterwork, the establishment of a protection zone of a water source, or an opinion on a notification, as well as the content particulars of the application and its annexes, and the particulars of decisions, measures of a general nature, binding opinions for the purposes of a joint land-use and building proceeding⁴⁾, consents, and opinions, in accordance with this Act.

(3) In cases where a decision of the water authority may affect water conditions in the territorial districts of several municipalities, the water authority shall announce the date and subject of an oral hearing by public notice also in these municipal offices.

(4) Municipalities in whose territorial district the water conditions or the environment may be affected by a decision of the water authority are also parties to the proceeding, unless this Act provides otherwise.

(5) The watercourse administrator is a party to the proceeding in cases where the proceeding concerns a watercourse.

(6) A citizens' association whose aim, according to its statutes, is the protection of the environment, is entitled to be informed about initiated administrative proceedings conducted under this Act, if it requests such information from the water authority, with the exception of building proceedings conducted under § 15 and proceedings following an environmental impact assessment under § 3 let. g) of the Environmental Impact Assessment Act; the request must be specified as to the subject matter and location of the proceeding. This request is valid for one year from the date of its submission and may be submitted repeatedly.

(7) A citizens' association has the status of a party to a proceeding conducted under this Act, with the exception of building proceedings conducted under § 15 and proceedings following an environmental impact assessment under § 3 let. g) of the Environmental Impact Assessment Act, if it requests in writing the status of a party to the proceeding within 8 days of the notification of the information under paragraph 6. The day of notification of the information on the initiation of the proceeding is understood as the day of delivery of its written version or the first day of its publication on the official notice board of the administrative authority and simultaneously in a manner enabling remote access.

(8) In a written document by which it sets the date and subject of an oral hearing, the water authority shall notify the parties to the proceeding and the authorities concerned at least 10 days before the oral hearing that they may submit binding opinions and objections, or possibly evidence, at the latest during the oral hearing, otherwise they will not be considered. If the water authority waives an oral hearing, it shall set a deadline, which may not be shorter than 10 days, by which the authorities concerned may submit binding opinions and the parties to the proceeding may submit their objections, or possibly evidence. No resolution is issued on the setting of the deadline. If it concerns decision-making related to waterworks, the procedure is according to the Building Act.

(9) In the case of a proceeding following an environmental impact assessment under § 3 let. g) of the Environmental Impact Assessment Act, it is a proceeding with a large number of participants. The holding of a public oral hearing is announced by a public notice, which must be posted at least 30 days in advance. Anyone may submit their comments at the latest during the public oral hearing, otherwise they will not be considered. If the water authority waives an oral hearing, it shall announce the initiation of the proceeding by a public notice, in which it shall set a deadline, which may not be shorter than 30 days from the posting of the notice, by which anyone may submit their comments. Comments submitted later will not be considered.

(10) If a decision affects water conditions or water quality in the district of another water authority or if a waterwork being decided upon is located partly in the district of another water authority, the substantively and locally competent water authority shall decide after consultation with those water authorities whose territorial districts are affected by the decision.

(11) In simple matters, especially if a decision can be made on the basis of documents submitted by the parties to the water management proceeding, the water authority shall decide without delay; the provisions of §§ 36 and 47 of the Administrative Procedure Code shall not apply, and if it is a proceeding ex officio, the decision may be the first act in the proceeding. In other cases, it shall decide no later than 60 days from the initiation of the water management proceeding; in particularly complex cases, no later than 3 months.

(12) If any of the conditions under § 140 para. 1 of the Administrative Procedure Code is met, it is a joint proceeding.

(13) If new decisive facts arise, the water authority may, in a new water management proceeding, change, or possibly revoke, even its other decisions issued in connection with a permit that has been changed or revoked.

(14) The costs of expert opinions that are needed in a water management proceeding initiated at the request of an applicant for a permit, or consent under this Act, shall be borne by the applicant.

(15) The provisions of §§ 12 and 13 shall apply mutatis mutandis to the issuance, amendment, revocation, or expiry of another decision of the water authority other than a permit for the management of waters.

(16) The applicant and persons under paragraphs 4 and 7 are parties to a proceeding for a permit for the abstraction of groundwater. The parties to a proceeding for the designation of an administrator of a minor watercourse or its revocation are the applicant, the existing administrator of the minor watercourse, the river basin administrator, and the municipalities through whose territory the minor watercourse flows. The relevant water authorities (§ 106 para. 1) shall provide an opinion on the issuance of the decision.

(17) When imposing remedial measures for deficiencies identified during water management supervision, the scope of which cannot be determined without prior surveys or the prior preparation of expert documents, the implementation of these surveys, or the preparation of said documents, may be imposed separately, and based on their results, the necessary remedial decisions may be issued separately. If a decision on remedial measures imposes the management of waters in a manner for which a permit under § 8 is otherwise required, this permit is no longer issued. If new decisive facts arise after the decision on remedial measures becomes final, a new decision on remedial measures may be issued.

(18) The manipulation rules of a waterwork are approved by the water authority by a decision.

(19) If a waterwork or activity extends into the administrative districts of several water authorities, the competent authority for the proceeding is the water authority in whose administrative district the decisive part of this waterwork is located or in whose administrative district the decisive part of the activity is to be carried out. An activity is understood as the management of waters, the activities listed in § 14, and other activities under the Act, including projects for which the water authority issues a binding opinion or an opinion under § 18. The locally competent authority for establishing the protection zones of a water source or a waterwork is the water authority in whose administrative district the waterwork with which the establishment of the protection zones is related is located.

(20) For the period of discussing a case in the special bodies established under international treaties by which the Czech Republic is bound, the deadlines for issuing a decision shall not run.

(21) In administrative proceedings conducted under § 8 para. 1 let. a) points 1, 2, 3, and 5, § 8 para. 1 let. b) points 1, 3, and 5, § 14 para. 1 let. b), d), e), and f), and under § 15 para. 1, the water authority shall assess the possibility of deteriorating the status or ecological potential of a surface water body or the status of a groundwater body or the impossibility of achieving good status or good ecological potential of a surface water body or good status of a groundwater body. If it concludes that the implementation of the project may lead to a deterioration of the status or ecological potential of a surface water body or a deterioration of the status of a groundwater body or prevent the achievement of good status or good ecological potential of a surface water body or good status of a groundwater body, it shall suspend the proceeding and inform the applicant that without an exemption under § 23a para. 8 it is not possible to permit or carry out the project.

§ 115a
Measure of a General Nature

(1) A measure of a general nature under § 6 para. 4, § 87k, and § 109 para. 1 is issued without a proceeding on the proposal for a measure of a general nature.

(2) A measure of a general nature under paragraph 1 becomes effective on the day of its posting on the official notice board of the authority competent to issue it. The measure of a general nature is also published on the official notice boards of the municipal offices in the municipalities whose administrative districts are affected by the measure of a general nature.

(3) The provision of § 172 para. 5 of the Administrative Procedure Code shall not be applied in the case of issuing a measure of a general nature under § 25 paras. 4 and 5 and § 66 para. 7.

(4) In the case of an amendment or revocation of a measure of a general nature, paragraphs 1 to 3 shall apply mutatis mutandis.

TITLE XV
OFFENSES

Division 1
Offenses of Natural Persons

§ 116

(1) A natural person commits an offense by
a) not complying with a decision or a measure of a general nature issued for the purpose of regulating, restricting, or prohibiting the general management of surface waters under § 6 para. 4,
b) managing surface or groundwaters under § 8 para. 1 without a permit for the management of waters,
c) carrying out an activity under § 14 para. 1 without a permit from the water authority or in violation of it,
d) in violation of § 16 para. 1 or 2, discharging, without a permit from the water authority, into a sewer system wastewater containing a particularly hazardous substance or a priority hazardous substance,
e) constructing a structure, facility, or carrying out an activity under § 17 para. 1 without the consent of the water authority or in violation of it,
f) violating the prohibition under § 28 para. 2,
g) violating the prohibition under § 30 para. 7 or 8,
h) not carrying out a technical measure or using lands or structures in violation of a measure of a general nature under § 30 para. 10,
i) not complying with the action programme in a vulnerable area under § 33 para. 2,
j) releasing fish or other aquatic animals of genetically unsuitable or unverified populations of native species into a watercourse or water reservoir in violation of § 35 para. 3,
k) not presenting documents on the removal of wastewater under § 38 para. 8,
l) in violation of § 39 para. 1, not taking appropriate measures when handling harmful substances to prevent them from entering surface or groundwaters, and thus endangering their environment,
m) violating the prohibition of washing a motor vehicle or operational machinery under § 39 para. 9,
n) violating the prohibition under § 46 para. 1 or 2,
o) violating the prohibition under § 58 para. 1 or the restriction under para. 3,
p) not fulfilling the obligation to ensure flood protection under § 63 para. 3,
q) violating the prohibition of activities in the active zone of a floodplain under § 67 para. 2,
r) in violation of § 87k para. 1, not fulfilling an obligation imposed by a measure of the drought commission during a state of water scarcity,
s) not providing information to a drought authority under § 87l para. 2,
t) managing waters in violation of a decision or a measure of a general nature under § 109 para. 1 or not carrying out a measure imposed under § 109 para. 2, or
u) not complying with a measure imposed under § 110 para. 1.

(2) A fine may be imposed for an offense under paragraph 1
a) up to CZK 20,000, for an offense under letters a), g), k), m), o), p), q), or s),
b) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under letters i), j), n), r), t), or u),
c) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under letters b), c), d), e), f), or h), or
d) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under letter l).

(3) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. b) committed by the abstraction of surface waters without a permit for the management of waters, a fine shall be imposed in the amount of the product of a rate of CZK 40 per 1 m³ of unlawfully abstracted surface water and the total quantity of this water, but not exceeding CZK 500,000.

(4) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. b) committed by the abstraction of groundwaters without a permit for the management of waters, a fine shall be imposed in the amount of the product of a rate of CZK 70 per 1 m³ of unlawfully abstracted groundwater and the total quantity of this water, but not exceeding CZK 500,000.

(5) A fine for an offense committed by the unauthorized abstraction of surface or groundwaters may be set for a maximum period of 3 years preceding the day on which the unauthorized water abstraction was discovered. The fine rate under paragraph 3 or 4 may be reduced if there are reasons of special consideration. However, a fine under paragraph 3 or 4 must not be assessed at a rate lower than CZK 10 per 1 m³ of unlawfully abstracted surface water or at a rate lower than CZK 15 per 1 m³ of unlawfully abstracted groundwater.

(6) If the quantity of surface or groundwaters abstracted without a permit for the management of waters or in violation of it cannot be determined, the authority imposing the fine shall determine the quantity of abstracted water according to the standard figures of annual water demand under the decree implementing the Act on Water Supply and Sewerage Systems⁴⁴ᵃ). If it is not possible to determine the quantity of abstracted water by such a procedure, the authority imposing the fine shall determine it by estimation; in doing so, it shall base its decision on the purpose of use of the abstracted water and local conditions.

§ 117
Violation of Obligations in the Use of Surface Waters for Navigation

(1) A natural person, as the operator of a vessel, commits an offense by
a) in violation of § 7 para. 2, not equipping a vessel with the necessary equipment for the accumulation of wastewater or not operating the equipment for the accumulation of wastewater properly, or not preventing the leakage of wastewater or harmful substances from vessels into surface waters, or
b) transferring wastewater or a harmful substance from a vessel or supplying a vessel with propellants or operating fluids in violation of § 7 para. 4.

(2) A natural person, as the master of a vessel, commits an offense by
a) using a vessel with a combustion engine for navigation on surface water in violation of § 7 para. 5, or
b) using a vessel for navigation in violation of the established scope and conditions of the use of surface waters for navigation under § 7 para. 5.

(3) A fine may be imposed for an offense under paragraphs 1 and 2
a) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a); however, if there is a leakage of wastewater or harmful substances into surface waters, a fine of up to CZK 200,000 may be imposed,
b) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. b),
c) up to CZK 200,000, for an offense under paragraph 2,
d) by an on-the-spot fine up to CZK 5,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. b).

§ 118
Violation of Other Obligations in the Management of Waters

(1) A natural person, as an authorized person, commits an offense by
a) managing surface or groundwaters under § 8 in violation of a permit for the management of waters,
b) not measuring the quantity of surface or groundwaters under § 10 para. 1 or 2, or not submitting the data to the relevant river basin administrator under § 22 para. 2, or
c) in violation of § 38 para. 6, not measuring the volume of discharged wastewater or the degree of its pollution, or not submitting the measurement results to the water authority.

(2) A natural person, as the acquirer of rights and obligations arising from a permit for the management of waters, with the exception of a permit for the abstraction of surface or groundwaters not exceeding 6,000 m³ annually or 500 m³ monthly, commits an offense by not notifying, under § 11 para. 1, the transfer or transition of the land or structure with which the permit for the management of waters is associated.

(3) A natural person, as the one who discharges wastewater into surface waters, commits an offense by
a) not allowing professionally competent persons under § 103 para. 5 to enter the premises where the controlled source of pollution is located, or not ensuring the conditions for carrying out the control, including the provision of the necessary documents for the control, or
b) not allowing the staff of the control laboratory under § 103a para. 5 to enter the premises where the source of pollution is located, or not ensuring the conditions for sampling from all outfalls of the controlled source of pollution.

(4) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 5,000, for an offense under paragraph 2,
b) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. b) or c) or paragraph 3, or
c) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a).

(5) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. a) committed by the abstraction of surface waters in violation of a permit for the management of waters, a fine shall be imposed in the amount specified under § 116 para. 3. The provisions of § 116 paras. 5 and 6 shall apply mutatis mutandis.

(6) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. a) committed by the abstraction of groundwaters in violation of a permit for the management of waters, a fine shall be imposed in the amount specified under § 116 para. 4. The provisions of § 116 paras. 5 and 6 shall apply mutatis mutandis.

§ 119
Violation of Obligations of Owners and Builders of Waterworks

(1) A natural person, as the owner or builder of a waterwork, commits an offense by
a) not maintaining the waterwork in proper condition under § 59 para. 1 let. b), or
b) not carrying out technical safety supervision under § 59 para. 1 let. c).

(2) A natural person, as the owner or builder of a waterwork of category I to IV, commits an offense by not fulfilling any of the obligations during the implementation of technical safety supervision under § 62 paras. 4 and 5.

(3) A natural person, as the owner or builder of a waterwork of category I or II, commits an offense by not discussing the implementation of securing works with the person authorized to carry out technical safety supervision under § 75 para. 3.

(4) A natural person, as the owner of a waterwork, commits an offense by
a) operating the waterwork in violation of § 59 para. 1 let. a),
b) failing to submit to the water authority for approval a proposal for the modification of the manipulation rules under § 59 para. 1 let. a),
c) disregarding the instructions of the watercourse administrator in case of extraordinary situations on the affected watercourse under § 59 para. 1 let. e),
d) failing to remove objects or materials attached to the waterwork under § 59 para. 1 let. f),
e) failing to install a benchmark, water mark, or water gauge, or failing to enable the continuous transmission of data on flows in the watercourse, or failing to ensure a special modification of the spillway or outlet under § 59 para. 1 let. g),
f) failing to install navigation signs under § 59 para. 1 let. h),
g) failing to carry out a technical review of the waterwork, failing to submit the results of the review to the water authority, or failing to remedy identified defects under § 59 para. 1 let. k),
h) failing to prepare or submit for approval the manipulation rules of the waterwork or a proposal for its supplementation, amendment, or modification under § 59 para. 3, or
i) failing to comply with an obligation in flood protection under § 84.

(5) A natural person, as the owner of a dike serving for flood protection, impoundment, or accumulation of surface waters, commits an offense by failing to remove volunteer trees under § 59 para. 1 let. j).

(6) A natural person, as the owner of a waterwork serving for the impoundment of water, commits an offense by
a) not maintaining the bed and banks of the watercourse in proper condition and not creating conditions for the migration of aquatic animals, unless it is a structure under § 59 para. 1 let. i), or
b) failing to notify the danger of a special flood or failing to warn, in case of imminent danger, the immediately threatened natural or legal persons under § 73 para. 3.

(7) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 20,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 or paragraph 4 let. f), g), h), i),
b) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 4 let. b), c), d), e), paragraph 5, or paragraph 6 let. a),
c) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. b), paragraph 3, or
d) up to CZK 1,000,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a), paragraph 4 let. a), or paragraph 6 let. b).

§ 120
Violation of Obligations of Owners of Lands, Structures, and Facilities

(1) A natural person, as the owner of land, commits an offense by failing to comply with an obligation under § 27.

(2) A natural person, as the owner of land on which a watercourse bed is located, commits an offense by failing to comply with an obligation under § 50.

(3) A natural person, as the owner of land adjacent to a watercourse bed, commits an offense by failing to comply with an obligation under § 51 para. 1.

(4) A natural person, as the owner of a structure or facility in a watercourse bed, commits an offense by failing, in violation of § 52 para. 1, to remove objects caught on or attached to the structure or facility.

(5) A natural person, as the owner of a structure that is not a waterwork, or a facility in a watercourse bed, commits an offense by failing, in violation of § 52 para. 2, to carry out remedial action for the disruption of the smooth flow of surface waters.

(6) A natural person, as the owner of land on which a structure for water management land improvements or its part is located, which is connected with more lands or was established in the public interest, and which was built before the effective date of this Act, commits an offense by
a) in violation of § 56 para. 4 let. a), not tolerating the structure for water management land improvements or its part,
b) using the land in violation of § 56 para. 4 let. b),
c) in violation of § 56 para. 4 let. c), failing to report to the owner of the structure for water management land improvements or to the water authority an apparent defect in its function, or
d) in violation of § 56 para. 4 let. d), not tolerating the use of the land for the maintenance of the structure for water management land improvements.

(7) A natural person, as the owner of land adjacent to a waterwork, commits an offense by not allowing entry or passage onto the land under § 60 para. 1.

(8) A natural person, as the owner or user of land or a structure or other premises, commits an offense by not allowing entry under § 21 para. 7 let. a).

(9) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 5,000, for an offense under paragraph 6 let. c) or paragraph 8,
b) up to CZK 10,000, for an offense under paragraph 6 let. b),
c) up to CZK 20,000, for an offense under paragraphs 1 to 3, paragraph 5, paragraph 6 let. a) and d), or paragraph 7, or
d) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 4.

§ 121
Violation of Obligations of Owners of Lands, Structures, and Facilities and Owners of Movable Property in Flood Protection

(1) A natural person, as the owner of land or a structure, commits an offense by failing, in violation of § 63 para. 3, to allow entry or passage onto their lands or structures for the purpose of ensuring flood protection.

(2) A natural person, as the owner of land or a structure located in a floodplain or that may worsen the course of a flood, commits an offense by
a) not having a prepared flood plan under § 71 para. 4 or 5, or
b) failing to comply with any of the obligations to prevent the worsening of runoff conditions or the course of a flood under § 85.

(3) A natural person, as the owner of an affected object, commits an offense by failing to ensure flood securing works on the affected object under § 75 para. 3.

(4) A natural person, as the owner of movable property, commits an offense by disregarding the placement or use of movable property under § 85 para. 3.

(5) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. a), paragraph 4, or
b) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 1, paragraph 2 let. b), or paragraph 3.

§ 122
Violation of Obligations in Handling Harmful Substances

(1) A natural person who is the holder of a permit for the discharge of wastewater containing a particularly hazardous substance or a priority hazardous substance into a sewer system commits an offense by
a) discharging wastewater containing a particularly hazardous substance or a priority hazardous substance into a sewer system in violation of a permit from the water authority under § 16 para. 1 or 2, or
b) in violation of a decision of the water authority under § 16 para. 4, failing to measure the volume of discharged wastewater or the degree of its pollution with particularly hazardous substances or priority hazardous substances, or failing to submit the measurement results.

(2) A natural person who handles harmful substances on a larger scale or where handling them is associated with an increased risk to surface or groundwaters commits an offense by
a) handling them without an approved contingency plan under § 39 para. 2 let. a), or
b) failing to keep or retain records of the measures taken under § 39 para. 2 let. b).

(3) A natural person who handles particularly hazardous substances or hazardous substances or who handles harmful substances on a larger scale or where handling them is associated with an increased risk commits an offense by failing to comply with any of the obligations under § 39 para. 4.

(4) A natural person who handles particularly hazardous substances commits an offense by failing to keep records or provide information under § 39 para. 6.

(5) A natural person commits an offense by acting in violation of an exemption under § 39 para. 7.

(6) A natural person commits an offense by supplementarily feeding fish with feed of plant origin in violation of § 39 para. 12.

(7) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 5,000, for an offense under paragraph 6,
b) up to CZK 20,000, for an offense under paragraph 5,
c) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 1, paragraph 2 let. b), or paragraph 4; if an offense under paragraph 1 is committed by discharging wastewater containing a particularly hazardous substance or a priority hazardous substance into a sewer system, a fine of up to CZK 500,000 may be imposed,
d) up to CZK 200,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. a), or
e) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 3.

(8) When determining the amount of the fine for an offense under paragraph 1, the authority imposing the fine shall take into account, in particular, the circumstances under which the unauthorized management occurred, how the natural person contributed to the removal or mitigation of the harmful consequences, the quantity and character of the leaked substance, the location where the actual endangerment occurred, the quantity and character of the harmful substance that penetrated into surface or groundwaters, the harmful consequences and the possibilities of their removal, and the effect of the harmful substance on the quality of these waters and the degree of protection of the affected area.

§ 123
Violation of Obligations during Accidents

(1) A natural person, as the originator of an accident, commits an offense by
a) failing to take immediate measures to eliminate the causes or consequences of the accident or, in its elimination, not following the approved contingency plan or the instructions of the water authority or the Czech Environmental Inspectorate under § 41 para. 1,
b) failing to immediately report the accident under § 41 para. 2, or
c) not complying with a call to cooperate in carrying out measures to eliminate the causes or consequences of the accident under § 41 para. 5.

(2) A natural person commits an offense during an accident by
a) failing to immediately report an accident they discovered under § 41 para. 2,
b) not providing requested data about the accident under § 41 para. 6, or
c) as a person on whom a remedial measure was imposed, failing to restore the land or structure that had to be used for the removal of the defective state to its previous state under § 42 para. 8.

(3) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. b),
b) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. c) or paragraph 2 let. a), c), or
c) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a) and b).

§ 124
Violation of Obligations of the Administrator of a Minor Watercourse

(1) A natural person, as the administrator of a minor watercourse or its section, commits an offense by
a) failing to comply with any of the obligations under § 47 para. 2,
b) failing to ensure flood securing works under § 75 para. 3, or
c) failing to comply with an obligation in flood protection under § 83.

(2) A fine may be imposed for an offense under paragraph 1
a) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under letter a), or
b) up to CZK 200,000, for an offense under letters b) and c).

§ 125
