Violation of Obligations of the Fee Payer

(1) A natural person, as a fee payer, commits an offense by failing, through an accredited laboratory, to take samples of wastewater or monitor the concentration of pollution in them for the relevant indicators according to Annex No. 2, part B, failing to determine the average concentration of individual pollutants, or failing to measure the volume of wastewater discharged from the source of pollution under § 89n para. 2.

(2) A fine of up to CZK 50,000 may be imposed for an offense under paragraph 1.

Division 2
Offenses of Legal Entities and Natural Persons Conducting Business

§ 125a

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business commits an offense by
a) not complying with a decision or a measure of a general nature issued for the purpose of regulating, restricting, or prohibiting the general management of surface waters under § 6 para. 4,
b) managing surface or groundwaters under § 8 para. 1 without a permit for the management of waters,
c) carrying out an activity under § 14 para. 1 without a permit from the water authority or in violation of it,
d) in violation of § 16 para. 1 or 2, discharging, without a permit from the water authority, into a sewer system wastewater containing a particularly hazardous substance or a priority hazardous substance,
e) constructing a structure, facility, or carrying out an activity under § 17 para. 1 without the consent of the water authority or in violation of it,
f) violating the prohibition under § 28 para. 2,
g) violating the prohibition under § 30 para. 7 or 8,
h) not carrying out a technical measure or using lands or structures in violation of a measure of a general nature under § 30 para. 10,
i) not complying with the action programme in a vulnerable area under § 33 para. 2,
j) releasing fish or other aquatic animals of genetically unsuitable or unverified populations of native species into a watercourse or water reservoir in violation of § 35 para. 3,
k) discharging mine water into surface or groundwaters in violation of § 38 para. 5,
l) not presenting documents on the removal of wastewater under § 38 para. 8,
m) in violation of § 39 para. 1, not taking appropriate measures when handling harmful substances to prevent them from entering surface or groundwaters, and thus endangering their environment,
n) violating the prohibition of washing a motor vehicle or operational machinery under § 39 para. 9,
o) violating the prohibition under § 46 para. 1,
p) violating the prohibition under § 58 para. 1 or the restriction under § 58 para. 3,
q) failing to comply with the obligation to ensure flood protection under § 63 para. 3,
r) violating the prohibition of activities in the active zone of a floodplain under § 67 para. 2,
s) in violation of § 87k para. 1, not fulfilling an obligation imposed by a measure of the drought commission during a state of water scarcity,
t) not providing information to a drought authority under § 87l para. 2,
u) discharging mine water without fulfilling the conditions set by the water authority or in violation of them,
v) managing waters in violation of a decision or a measure of a general nature under § 109 para. 1 or not carrying out a measure imposed under § 109 para. 2, or
w) not complying with a measure imposed under § 110 para. 1 or § 112 para. 1 let. b).

(2) A fine may be imposed for an offense under paragraph 1
a) up to CZK 20,000, for an offense under letters a), g), p), or q),
b) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under letter t),
c) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under letters f), i), j), k), l), n), r), s), or v),
d) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under letters b), c), e), h), o), or w),
e) up to CZK 1,000,000, for an offense under letters m) or u), or
f) up to CZK 5,000,000, for an offense under letter d).

(3) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. b) committed by discharging wastewater into surface or groundwaters without a permit for the management of waters, a fine of up to CZK 5,000,000 may be imposed.

(4) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. b) committed by the abstraction of surface waters without a permit for the management of waters, a fine may be imposed in the amount of the product of a rate of CZK 40 per 1 m³ of unlawfully abstracted surface water and the total quantity of this water, but not exceeding CZK 10,000,000.

(5) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. b) committed by the abstraction of groundwaters without a permit for the management of waters, a fine may be imposed in the amount of the product of a rate of CZK 70 per 1 m³ of unlawfully abstracted groundwater and the total quantity of this water, but not exceeding CZK 10,000,000.

(6) A fine for an offense committed by the unauthorized abstraction of surface or groundwaters may be set for a maximum period of 3 years preceding the day on which the unauthorized water abstraction was discovered. The fine rate under paragraph 4 or 5 may be reduced if there are reasons of special consideration. However, a fine under paragraph 4 or 5 must not be assessed at a rate lower than CZK 10 per 1 m³ of unlawfully abstracted surface water or at a rate lower than CZK 15 per 1 m³ of unlawfully abstracted groundwater.

(7) If the quantity of surface or groundwaters abstracted without a permit for the management of waters or in violation of it cannot be determined, the authority imposing the fine shall determine the quantity of abstracted water according to the standard figures of annual water demand under the decree implementing the Act on Water Supply and Sewerage Systems⁴⁴ᵃ). If it is not possible to determine the quantity of abstracted water by such a procedure, the authority imposing the fine shall determine it by estimation; in doing so, it shall base its decision on the purpose of use of the abstracted water and local conditions.

§ 125b
Violation of Obligations in the Use of Surface Waters for Navigation

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the operator of a vessel, commits an offense by
a) in violation of § 7 para. 2, not equipping a vessel with the necessary equipment for the accumulation of wastewater or not operating the equipment for the accumulation of wastewater properly, or not preventing the leakage of wastewater or harmful substances from vessels into surface waters,
b) not ensuring the obligations of the operator of a special vessel intended for the transport of fuel and waste from vessels under § 7 para. 3,
c) transferring wastewater or a harmful substance from a vessel or supplying a vessel with propellants or operating fluids in violation of § 7 para. 4,
d) using a vessel with a combustion engine for navigation on surface water in violation of § 7 para. 5, or
e) using a vessel for navigation in violation of the established scope and conditions of the use of surface waters for navigation under § 7 para. 5.

(2) The operator of a port, a special service facility, or a service vessel commits an offense by, in violation of § 7 para. 3, supplying vessels with propellants and operating fluids or removing wastewater or harmful substances from vessels in ports or by means of special service facilities of service vessels in such a way that the pollution of surface or groundwaters is not excluded.

(3) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a); however, if there is a leakage of wastewater or harmful substances into surface waters, a fine of up to CZK 200,000 may be imposed,
b) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. c), or
c) up to CZK 200,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. b), d), e), or paragraph 2.

§ 125c
Violation of Other Obligations in the Management of Waters

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as an authorized person, commits an offense by
a) managing surface or groundwaters under § 8 in violation of a permit for the management of waters,
b) not measuring the quantity of surface or groundwaters under § 10 para. 1 or 2, or not submitting the data to the relevant river basin administrator under § 22 para. 2, or
c) in violation of § 38 para. 6, not measuring the volume of discharged wastewater or the degree of its pollution, or not submitting the measurement results to the water authority.

(2) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the acquirer of rights and obligations arising from a permit for the management of waters, with the exception of a permit for the abstraction of surface or groundwaters not exceeding 6,000 m³ annually or 500 m³ monthly, commits an offense by not notifying, under § 11 para. 1, the transfer of the land or structure with which the permit for the management of waters is associated.

(3) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as a person carrying out the removal of wastewater accumulated in a sealed tank, commits an offense by not issuing a document to the person who accumulates this water, under § 38 para. 8.

(4) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the one who discharges wastewater into surface waters, commits an offense by
a) not allowing professionally competent persons under § 103 para. 5 to enter the premises where the controlled source of pollution is located, or not ensuring the conditions for carrying out the control, including the provision of the necessary documents for the control, or
b) not allowing the staff of the control laboratory under § 103a para. 5 to enter the premises where the source of pollution is located, or not ensuring the conditions for sampling from all outfalls of the controlled source of pollution.

(5) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 5,000, for an offense under paragraph 2,
b) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. b) or c) or paragraph 3 or 4, or
c) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a).

(6) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. a) committed by discharging wastewater into surface or groundwaters in violation of a permit for the management of waters, a fine of up to CZK 5,000,000 may be imposed.

(7) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. a) committed by the abstraction of surface waters in violation of a permit for the management of waters, a fine shall be imposed in the amount specified under § 125a para. 4. The provisions of § 125a paras. 6 and 7 shall apply mutatis mutandis.

(8) For an offense under paragraph 1 let. a) committed by the abstraction of groundwaters in violation of a permit for the management of waters, a fine shall be imposed in the amount specified under § 125a para. 5. The provisions of § 125a paras. 6 and 7 shall apply mutatis mutandis.

§ 125d
Violation of Obligations of Owners and Builders of Waterworks

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner or builder of a waterwork, commits an offense by not maintaining the waterwork in proper condition under § 59 para. 1 let. b).

(2) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner or builder of a waterwork of category I to IV, commits an offense by not carrying out technical safety supervision under § 59 para. 1 let. c).

(3) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner or builder of a waterwork of category I to IV, commits an offense by failing to comply with any of the obligations during the implementation of technical safety supervision under § 62 paras. 4 and 5.

(4) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner or builder of a waterwork of category I or II, commits an offense by not discussing the implementation of securing works with the person authorized to carry out technical safety supervision under § 75 para. 3.

(5) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of a waterwork, commits an offense by
a) operating the waterwork in violation of § 59 para. 1 let. a),
b) failing to submit to the water authority for approval a proposal for the modification of the manipulation rules under § 59 para. 1 let. a),
c) disregarding the instructions of the watercourse administrator in case of extraordinary situations on the affected watercourse under § 59 para. 1 let. e),
d) failing to remove objects or materials attached to the waterwork under § 59 para. 1 let. f),
e) failing to install a benchmark, water mark, or water gauge, or failing to enable the continuous transmission of data on flows in the watercourse, or failing to ensure a special modification of the spillway or outlet under § 59 para. 1 let. g),
f) failing to install navigation signs under § 59 para. 1 let. h),
g) failing to carry out a technical review of the waterwork, failing to submit the results of the review to the water authority, or failing to remedy identified defects under § 59 para. 1 let. k),
h) failing to prepare or submit for approval the manipulation rules of the waterwork or a proposal for its supplementation, amendment, or modification under § 59 para. 3, or
i) failing to comply with an obligation in flood protection under § 84.

(6) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of a dike serving for flood protection, impoundment, or accumulation of surface waters, commits an offense by failing to remove volunteer trees under § 59 para. 1 let. j).

(7) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of a waterwork serving for the impoundment of water, commits an offense by
a) not maintaining the bed and banks of the watercourse in proper condition and not creating conditions for the migration of aquatic animals, unless it is a structure under § 59 para. 1 let. i), or
b) failing to notify the danger of a special flood, or failing to warn, in case of imminent danger, the immediately threatened natural or legal persons under § 73 para. 3.

(8) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 20,000, for an offense under paragraph 3 or paragraph 5 let. f), g), h),
b) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 5 let. b), c), d), e), i), paragraph 6, or paragraph 7 let. a),
c) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 or paragraph 4, or
d) up to CZK 1,000,000, for an offense under paragraph 1, paragraph 5 let. a), or paragraph 7 let. b).

§ 125e
Violation of Obligations of Owners of Lands, Structures, and Facilities

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of land, commits an offense by failing to comply with an obligation under § 27.

(2) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of land on which a watercourse bed is located, commits an offense by failing to comply with an obligation under § 50.

(3) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of land adjacent to a watercourse bed, commits an offense by failing to comply with an obligation under § 51 para. 1.

(4) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of a structure or facility in a watercourse bed, commits an offense by failing, in violation of § 52 para. 1, to remove objects caught on or attached to the structure or facility.

(5) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of a structure that is not a waterwork, or a facility in a watercourse bed, commits an offense by failing, in violation of § 52 para. 2, to carry out remedial action for the disruption of the smooth flow of surface waters.

(6) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of land on which a structure for water management land improvements or its part is located, which is connected with more lands or was established in the public interest, and which was built before the effective date of this Act, commits an offense by
a) in violation of § 56 para. 4 let. a), not tolerating the structure for water management land improvements or its part,
b) using the land in violation of § 56 para. 4 let. b),
c) in violation of § 56 para. 4 let. c), failing to report to the owner of the structure for water management land improvements or to the water authority an apparent defect in its function, or
d) in violation of § 56 para. 4 let. d), not tolerating the use of the land for the maintenance of the structure for water management land improvements.

(7) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of land adjacent to a waterwork, commits an offense by not allowing entry or passage onto the land under § 60 para. 1.

(8) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner or user of land or a structure or other premises, commits an offense by not allowing entry under § 21 para. 7 let. a).

(9) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 20,000, for an offense under paragraph 6 let. c) or paragraph 8,
b) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 3 or paragraph 6 let. b),
c) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 1, paragraph 2, paragraph 5, paragraph 6 let. a), d), or paragraph 7, or
d) up to CZK 200,000, for an offense under paragraph 4.

§ 125f
Violation of Obligations of Owners of Lands, Structures, and Facilities and Owners of Movable Property in Flood Protection

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of land or a structure, commits an offense by failing, in violation of § 63 para. 3, to allow entry or passage onto the lands or structures for the purpose of ensuring flood protection.

(2) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of land or a structure located in a floodplain or that may worsen the course of a flood, commits an offense by
a) not having a prepared flood plan under § 71 para. 4 or 5, or
b) failing to comply with any of the obligations to prevent the worsening of runoff conditions or the course of a flood under § 85.

(3) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of an affected object, commits an offense by failing to ensure flood securing works on the affected object under § 75 para. 3.

(4) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the owner of movable property, commits an offense by disregarding the placement or use of movable property under § 85 para. 3.

(5) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. a), paragraph 4, or
b) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 1, paragraph 2 let. b), or paragraph 3.

§ 125g
Violation of Obligations in Handling Harmful Substances

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business who is the holder of a permit for the discharge of wastewater containing a particularly hazardous substance or a priority hazardous substance into a sewer system commits an offense by
a) discharging wastewater containing a particularly hazardous substance or a priority hazardous substance into a sewer system in violation of a permit from the water authority under § 16 para. 1 or 2,
b) in violation of a decision of the water authority under § 16 para. 4, failing to measure the volume of discharged wastewater or the degree of its pollution with particularly hazardous substances or priority hazardous substances, or failing to submit the measurement results.

(2) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business who handles harmful substances on a larger scale or where handling them is associated with an increased risk to surface or groundwaters commits an offense by
a) handling them without an approved contingency plan under § 39 para. 2 let. a), or
b) failing to keep or retain records of the measures taken under § 39 para. 2 let. b).

(3) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business who handles particularly hazardous substances or hazardous substances or who handles harmful substances on a larger scale or where handling them is associated with an increased risk commits an offense by failing to comply with any of the obligations under § 39 para. 4.

(4) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business who handles particularly hazardous substances commits an offense by failing to keep records or provide information under § 39 para. 6.

(5) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business commits an offense by acting in violation of an exemption under § 39 para. 7.

(6) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business commits an offense by supplementarily feeding fish with feed of plant origin in violation of § 39 para. 12.

(7) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 30,000, for an offense under paragraph 6,
b) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 5,
c) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. b), paragraph 2 let. b), or paragraph 4,
d) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. a),
e) up to CZK 1,000,000, for an offense under paragraph 3, or
f) up to CZK 5,000,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a).

(8) When determining the amount of the fine for an offense under paragraph 1, the authority imposing the fine shall take into account, in particular, the circumstances under which the unauthorized management occurred, how the legal entity or natural person conducting business contributed to the removal or mitigation of the harmful consequences, the quantity and character of the leaked substance, the location where the actual endangerment occurred, the quantity and character of the harmful substance that penetrated into surface or groundwaters, the harmful consequences and the possibilities of their removal, and the effect of the harmful substance on the quality of these waters and the degree of protection of the affected area.

§ 125h
Violation of Obligations during Accidents

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the originator of an accident, commits an offense by
a) failing to take immediate measures to eliminate the causes or consequences of the accident or, in its elimination, not following the approved contingency plan or the instructions of the water authority or the Czech Environmental Inspectorate under § 41 para. 1,
b) failing to immediately report the accident under § 41 para. 2, or
c) not complying with a call to cooperate in carrying out measures to eliminate the causes or consequences of the accident under § 41 para. 5.

(2) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business commits an offense during an accident by
a) failing to immediately report an accident they discovered under § 41 para. 2,
b) not providing requested data about the accident under § 41 para. 6, or
c) as a person on whom a remedial measure was imposed, failing to restore the land or structure that had to be used for the removal of the defective state to its previous state under § 42 para. 8.

(3) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. b),
b) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. c) or paragraph 2 let. a), c), or
c) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a) and b).

§ 125i
Violation of Obligations of the Watercourse Administrator and River Basin Administrator

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the administrator of a minor watercourse, commits an offense by
a) failing to comply with any of the obligations under § 47 para. 2,
b) failing to ensure flood securing works under § 75 para. 3, or
c) failing to comply with an obligation in flood protection under § 83.

(2) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as the administrator of a significant watercourse, commits an offense by
a) failing to comply with any of the obligations under § 47 para. 2,
b) failing to ensure flood securing works under § 75 para. 3, or
c) failing to comply with an obligation in flood protection under § 83.

(3) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as a river basin administrator, commits an offense by failing to comply with an obligation in flood protection under § 82.

(4) A fine may be imposed for an offense
a) up to CZK 50,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. a),
b) up to CZK 100,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. a),
c) up to CZK 200,000, for an offense under paragraph 1 let. b), c), or
d) up to CZK 500,000, for an offense under paragraph 2 let. b), c), or paragraph 3.

§ 125j
Violation of the Obligation of a Municipality

(1) A municipality commits an offense by failing to submit an application for a land-use decision under § 92 of the Building Act for the purpose of fulfilling the obligation set in Art. II, point 6 of Act No. 20/2004 Coll.

(2) A fine of up to CZK 1,000,000 may be imposed for this offense.

§ 125k
Violation of the Obligation of the Fee Payer

(1) A legal entity or a natural person conducting business, as a fee payer, commits an offense by failing, through an accredited laboratory, to take samples of wastewater or monitor the concentration of pollution in them for the relevant indicators according to Annex No. 2, part B, failing to determine the average concentration of individual pollutants, or failing to measure the volume of wastewater discharged from the source of pollution under § 89n para. 2.

(2) A fine of up to CZK 100,000 may be imposed for an offense under paragraph 1.

Division 3
Common Provisions on Offenses

§ 125l

(1) The Czech Environmental Inspectorate or the water authority may also waive the imposition of an administrative penalty if the perpetrator of the offense takes factual measures to remedy the consequences of the violation of the obligation, as well as measures to prevent further endangerment or pollution of ground or surface waters, and the imposition of an administrative penalty would, given the costs of the measures taken, lead to disproportionate hardship.

(2) The rate of a fine for an offense under this Act is doubled, but not exceeding CZK 20,000,000, if the same offense is committed repeatedly. An offense is committed repeatedly if, from the date the decision on the imposition of a fine for the same offense became final, 1 year has not elapsed.

(3) When determining the amount of the fine for an offense committed by discharging wastewater without a permit for the management of waters or in violation of it, the authority imposing the fine shall take into account, in particular, the degree of exceeding the conditions of the permit for the discharge of this water, the degree of impact on the quality of surface or groundwaters and its local extent, the degree of protection of the affected area, and the cause of the unauthorized discharge.

(4) An offense under § 125j is prosecuted by the Czech Environmental Inspectorate. Administrative offenses under § 117 para. 2 and § 125b para. 1 let. d) and e) are prosecuted by the State Navigation Administration. Other offenses under this Act are prosecuted within the scope of their powers by the water authority or the Czech Environmental Inspectorate. A fine for an offense under § 117 para. 2 let. b) may be imposed on the spot by the State Navigation Administration and the authority of the Police of the Czech Republic. The offense is prosecuted by the one of the competent administrative authorities that initiated the proceeding first, or if the proceeding was initiated on the same day, then by the water authority or the State Navigation Administration.

(5) For a violation of obligations established by building regulations and concerning waterworks, fines are imposed by the water authorities within the scope of their powers under a special act.⁴)

(6) Fines imposed by the Czech Environmental Inspectorate on municipalities and by the State Navigation Administration are revenue for the State Environmental Fund. Other fines imposed by the Czech Environmental Inspectorate are 50% revenue for the budget of the municipality in whose territorial district the offense was committed, and 50% revenue for the State Environmental Fund of the Czech Republic.

TITLE XVI
COMMON AND TRANSITIONAL PROVISIONS

§ 126
Common Provisions

(1) If this Act uses the term "owner" or "acquirer," it is also understood as the one to whom the right of management pertains. If the owner has transferred the rights or obligations to which the relevant provision applies to a user, the user is considered the owner.

(2) Administrators of watercourses, if they are state organizations, are obliged, at the request, to take over from the relevant state organizational units the waterworks on the watercourses and the lands forming the beds of the watercourses in the sections they administer, from these state organizational units, if they manage the said property under a special act because, when it was acquired by the state, it was not apparent to which organizational unit or state organization the management thereof pertains, or it was found to be the property of the state, but no state organizational unit or state organization manages it.⁴⁵) In case of doubt as to which administrator is to take over the waterwork or land of the state, such an administrator shall be designated by the Ministry of Agriculture; this designation does not have the nature of a decision in an administrative proceeding.

(3) A detailed drainage facility owned by the state located on foreign land becomes, including the relevant technical documentation, if available, the property of the owner of the land affected by this structure, and a detailed drainage facility built by the state on land that is state-owned passes, in the event of the transfer of this land, to the ownership of the new acquirer free of charge together with the land, unless they notify the relevant water authority within 24 months of the effective date of this Act that they do not consent to the transfer. The transfer of these ownership rights occurs on the day following the expiry of the deadline for claiming non-consent to the transfer.

(4) The powers of water authorities not expressly stated must be assessed according to the areas in which the performance of state administration pertains to them.

(5) Decisions issued under § 8 para. 1, § 12 para. 1, § 16 para. 1, § 17 para. 1, § 39 para. 2 let. a) are not issued under this Act if their issuance is replaced by a procedure in a proceeding for the issuance of an integrated permit under the Act on integrated prevention and pollution control, on the integrated pollution register, and on the amendment of certain acts (the Integrated Prevention Act). Other provisions of this Act, including the time limitation of the validity of the permitted management of waters, are not affected by this and must be taken into account in the procedure under the Integrated Prevention Act, with the exception of the requirement for the simultaneous issuance of a decision under § 9 para. 5. The person to whom a right from a decision issued under the Integrated Prevention Act pertains is considered an authorized person under the Water Act (§ 8 para. 2). The issuance of a decision under § 17 para. 1 is not replaced by a procedure in a proceeding for the issuance of an integrated permit under the Integrated Prevention Act if the integrated permit is issued at the request of the facility operator after the issuance of a building permit or a joint permit by which the construction is located and permitted, under a special act.⁴)

(6) The reporting obligation towards water authorities or authorized subjects under § 10 para. 1, § 22 para. 2, § 38 para. 6 for sources of pollution with a permitted quantity of discharged wastewater greater than 6,000 m³/year is fulfilled through the integrated system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment or a data box of the ministry designated for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment under the Act on the integrated pollution register and the integrated system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment and on the amendment of certain acts.

(7) A remedial measure under § 42, § 110 para. 1, § 111 para. 2, or § 112 para. 1 let. b) shall not be imposed if a decision on the imposition of a remedial measure has been issued for the remedying of environmental damage to surface or groundwaters under the Act on the prevention and remedying of environmental damage and on the amendment of certain acts⁴⁵ᵃ). An initiated proceeding for the imposition of a remedial measure under § 42, § 110 para. 1, § 111 para. 2, or § 112 para. 1 let. b) shall be suspended by the water authority or the Czech Environmental Inspectorate if a proceeding for the imposition of a remedial measure has been initiated for the remedying of environmental damage to surface or groundwaters under the Act on the prevention and remedying of environmental damage and on the amendment of certain acts⁴⁵ᵃ).

(8) In proceedings under § 3 para. 3, § 8 para. 4, § 12 para. 1, § 38 para. 15, § 43 para. 2, § 44 para. 3, § 53, § 55 para. 4, § 56 para. 5, § 61 para. 9, § 64 para. 2, and § 71 para. 4, the water authority shall decide ex officio.

(9) If this Act uses the term building permit, it is also understood as a joint permit by which a construction is located and permitted under a special act.⁴)

§ 126a

The powers assigned to the regional authority, the municipal office of a municipality with extended powers, an authorized municipal office, or a municipal office, as well as their flood commissions and drought commissions, are the exercise of delegated powers.

§ 126b

(1) The sampling and analysis of wastewater under § 38 para. 6 or § 103a and the control of the correctness of the measurement of the volume of discharged wastewater under § 103 paras. 1 and 2 may be temporarily⁴⁵ᵇ⁾ carried out in the territory of the Czech Republic also by persons established in other member states of the European Union, if
a) they are nationals of the member states of the European Union, and
b) they are authorized to carry out the activities listed in § 38 para. 6, § 103 para. 1 and 2, or § 103a under the legal regulations of other member states of the European Union.

(2) These persons are obliged to present documents on the fulfillment of the conditions under paragraph 1 let. a) and b) to the person who discharges wastewater into surface waters before commencing the activities listed in paragraph 1.

§ 127
Transitional Provisions

(1) Rights and obligations established by previous legal regulations shall remain preserved, unless this Act provides otherwise. Proceedings initiated and not concluded before the effective date of this Act shall be concluded according to the previous regulations.

(2) When imposing an increased fine, fines imposed under previous legal regulations are considered fines imposed under this Act.

(3) The classification of waterworks into categories for the purposes of technical safety supervision (§ 61) under previous legal regulations remains in force.

(4) An authorization granted for the performance of technical safety supervision under previous legal regulations is considered an authorization granted for the performance of technical safety supervision under this Act, provided that the conditions for the performance of technical safety supervision under which the authorization was granted have not changed on the part of the authorized person.

(5) Ownership rights to lands that form the beds of watercourses, which are not yet registered in the Real Estate Cadastre as parcels with the land type of water body and which became state property under Act No. 138/1973 Coll., on waters (the Water Act), as amended, shall pass to the owners of the lands registered in the Real Estate Cadastre on which these beds are located, unless they notify the relevant water authority within 6 months of the effective date of this Act that they do not consent to the transfer. The transfer of these ownership rights occurs on the day following the expiry of the deadline for claiming non-consent to the transfer.

(6) If municipalities, at the time of the entry into force of this Act, discharge wastewater into surface waters in violation of the provisions of this Act, the water authority may, at their request submitted within 3 months of the effective date of this Act, issue a new permit for the discharge of wastewater, up to the level of pollution in the discharged wastewater in the period of the last 12 months before the effective date of this Act. This new permit replaces the existing valid permit as of the effective date of this Act. The water authority shall, in the new permit, set a reasonable deadline within which the indicators and permissible values of wastewater pollution, which will be in accordance with this Act and the regulations issued thereunder, will be achieved, and the conditions for the gradual achievement of the required level of discharged pollution; when setting the deadline, the water authority shall take into account the justified requirements of water protection and the possibilities of a technical solution. For this period, the water authority or the Czech Environmental Inspectorate shall refrain from imposing fines under § 116 para. 1 let. b) on the assumption that the conditions for achieving the required level of discharged pollution are being met. The reasonable deadline within which the indicators and permissible values of wastewater pollution, which will be in accordance with this Act and the regulations issued thereunder, will be achieved, and the conditions for the gradual achievement of the required level of discharged pollution, may not be set by the water authority for sources of pollution above 2,000 population equivalents longer than until December 31, 2010.

(7) Abstractions of groundwater, or possibly surface water, that are mine waters, are considered permitted from the effective date of this Act; this permit is valid until December 31, 2004, unless their further abstraction is permitted under § 8. During the above-mentioned period, the provisions on fees under Title X of this Act do not apply to these abstractions.

(8) The documents necessary to ensure the administration of fees for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters under this Act shall be handed over by the Czech Environmental Inspectorate to the regional authorities in their delegated capacity no later than 30 days from the date of their establishment.

(9) The water management records under previous legal regulations become part of the records of decisions of water authorities under § 19.

(10) The discharge of water into public sewer systems, the supply of water from public water supply systems, and water and sewerage charges are governed by the previous legal regulations, including §§ 24, 30, and 46 of Act No. 138/1973 Coll., on waters (the Water Act), as amended, until a new legal regulation on water supply and sewerage systems comes into force.

(11) Fees calculated according to the rates specified in part B of Annex No. 2 to this Act shall be paid for the year 2002 at only 80% of their amount.

(12) Fees calculated according to the rates specified in part A of Annex No. 2 to this Act shall be paid for the year 2002 for the purpose of drinking water supply and for the purpose of other use not yet charged under a special legal regulation⁴⁶) at 35% of their amount, and for the year 2003 at 70% of their amount.

(13) Water management works permitted under previous legal regulations are considered waterworks under this Act. If the term "water management work" is used in other legal regulations, it is understood as a waterwork under this Act.

(14) The rights and obligations established under previous legal regulations in the area of fees for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters and payments for the abstraction of surface or groundwaters shall remain in force even after the effective date of this Act.

(15) Water authorities are obliged, in their decision-making, issuance of opinions, and in the implementation of other measures under this Act, to be guided by the indicative water management plan in its valid version until the approval of new plans under this Act in the relevant river basin district.

(16) Inundation areas established under previous legal regulations are considered floodplains under § 66.

(17) Administrators of minor watercourses designated under previous legal regulations are considered administrators of minor watercourses under this Act.

PART TWO
Amendment to the Act on the Protection of Public Health

§ 128

Act No. 258/2000 Coll., on the protection of public health and on the amendment of certain related acts, is amended as follows:

In § 4, paragraph 3, including footnote No. 7), shall read:
"(3) To the minimum extent and frequency, determined by an implementing legal regulation, the person specified in § 3 para. 2, with the exception of the owner and administrator of a public water supply, is obliged to ensure the control of drinking water in an accredited laboratory⁷) or in an authorized laboratory (§ 83a). The scope and frequency of the control may be adjusted by the public health protection authority competent according to the place of activity, at the request of the person, by a decision.
⁷) Act No. 22/1997 Coll., as amended.".

In § 80 para. 1, a comma is inserted after letter l) and letter m) is added, which reads:
"m) grants and revokes authorization for the performance of authorization.".

After § 83, new §§ 83a to 83d are inserted, which, including footnote No. 47a), read:
"§ 83a
(1) For the purposes of this Act, authorization is understood as a procedure initiated at the request of a natural person who is an entrepreneur, or a legal person, on the basis of which a certificate is issued that the person is competent in a defined scope to carry out
a) sampling and testing of the quality and health safety of drinking water (§ 3 para. 1), water in swimming pools, and water at the source for an artificial swimming pool or sauna (§ 6),
b) determining and measuring the concentrations and intensities of factors in the internal environment of buildings (§ 13 para. 1),
c) sampling and measuring microbial and parasitic contamination of outdoor play areas (§ 13 para. 2),
d) sampling and testing the health safety of products coming into direct contact with drinking and raw water, with the exception of construction products (§ 5), and consumer products, with the exception of toys (§ 25),
e) control of disinfection and sterilization (§ 17),
f) sampling and testing the health safety of food [§ 24 para. 1 let. e)],
g) determining and measuring the intensity of noise, vibrations, and non-ionizing radiation in the municipal and working environment (§§ 30 to 35),
h) determining and measuring the intensity of lighting and microclimatic conditions and the concentration of dust and chemical pollutants in the working environment (§ 37 para. 3),
i) biological exposure tests and testing in the field of genetic toxicology, physiology, and psychology of work.
(2) The Ministry of Health may entrust the performance of authorization to a legal person or an organizational unit of the state, established to fulfill tasks within the competence of the Ministry of Health (hereinafter "authorizing body"). This entrustment is non-transferable. The Administrative Procedure Code does not apply to the issuance of this entrustment. The authorization is carried out according to the conditions set by the Ministry of Health for individual areas under paragraph 1. The entrustment of an authorizing body and the revocation of this entrustment, as well as the conditions for authorization, shall be published by the Ministry of Health in the Bulletin of the Ministry of Health.
§ 83b
(1) The authorizing body shall issue a certificate of authorization to a legal person or a natural person who is an entrepreneur, at their request. This certificate shall be issued if the applicant meets the conditions for authorization, which are
a) professional level in relation to the proposed area of authorization,
b) equipment for technical and administrative acts and accessibility to facilities for special investigations,
c) the existence of the necessary number of employees with professional training, knowledge, and skills,
d) the existence of a commitment of the employees to confidentiality about facts of which the persons carrying out the authorization become aware,
e) the absence of financial or other interests that could influence the results of the activities of the person carrying out the authorization,
f) the integrity of the applicant for authorization.
(2) The absence of financial or other interests under paragraph 1 let. e) is proven by a solemn declaration.
(3) For the purposes of this Act, a person who has been finally convicted of a criminal offense whose factual basis is related to the object of business is not considered to be of integrity. Integrity under paragraph 1 let. f) is proven for a legal person by its statutory representative and all members of the statutory body. A natural person proves their integrity with an extract from the Criminal Register, which must not be older than 3 months.
(4) In the application for the issuance of a certificate of authorization, the applicant shall state the business name, the name and surname of the natural person or the name of the legal person, the place of business, or possibly the permanent residence, if it is a natural person, the registered office of the legal person, the identification number, and further data proving the fulfillment of the conditions under paragraph 1. A foreign person⁴⁷ᵃ⁾ shall state their residence outside the territory of the Czech Republic, the place of stay in the Czech Republic, if the stay has been permitted, the location and designation of the organizational unit in the territory of the Czech Republic, the name and surname of the head of the organizational unit and the address of their stay in the territory of the Czech Republic, and further data proving the fulfillment of the conditions under paragraph 1.
(5) Citizens of the member states of the European Union prove their entitlement to perform authorization under § 83a para. 1 by
a) a proof of competence required in a member state of the European Union for access to these activities and issued by this member state of the European Union, or
b) a document proving the qualification for the performance of these activities obtained in a member state of the European Union,
if they provide guarantees, especially in the areas of health, safety, environmental protection, and consumer protection to the extent regulated in § 83a para. 1.
(6) In case of doubt, the Ministry of Health decides on the fulfillment of the requirements under paragraph 5 at the request of a citizen of a member state of the European Union. The application must contain documents issued by the relevant authorities of a member state of the European Union, proving the facts stated in paragraph 5. The proceeding on the assessment of the application must be concluded no later than 4 months after the submission of all documents relating to the person concerned.
§ 83c
(1) The certificate of authorization defines the subject matter, scope, and conditions of the activity and the period for which it was issued. The Administrative Procedure Code does not apply to the issuance of a certificate of authorization. The applicant may file objections against the notification of the non-issuance of a certificate of authorization within 3 days of its delivery. The Ministry of Health decides on the objections. An appeal against the decision of the Ministry of Health on the objections is not possible. The costs associated with the authorization, including the issuance of the certificate of authorization, are borne by the applicant. The price is negotiated according to a special legal regulation.
(2) Authorization is non-transferable to another person and is granted for a period of no more than 5 years from the date of granting. The authorization may be extended for another 5 years each time. The application for the extension of the validity of the certificate of authorization must be submitted by the person to whom the certificate of authorization was issued (hereinafter "the holder of the authorization") to the authorizing body at least 6 months before the end of the validity of the certificate.
(3) A list of the holders of authorization with the business name, registered office, or possibly place of business, and identification number under § 83b para. 4, as well as changes in these data, shall be published by the Ministry of Health in the Bulletin of the Ministry of Health. This data is communicated to the Ministry of Health by the authorizing body.
(4) The holder of the authorization is obliged to comply with the conditions of authorization and to participate in interlaboratory tests in the term and scope determined by the authorizing body. The holder of the authorization must keep documents on the results of interlaboratory tests for a period of 5 years. The costs associated with the interlaboratory tests are borne by the holder of the authorization.
(5) The authorizing body controls compliance with the conditions of authorization and the results of interlaboratory tests. For this purpose, it is entitled to enter the premises of the holder of the authorization, to verify the fulfillment of the conditions of authorization, and to request the submission of documents, including the results of interlaboratory tests. The authorizing body may invite an expert for the relevant area to the control. If the authorizing body finds deficiencies, depending on the severity of the deficiencies, it shall suspend the validity of the certificate or withdraw it. The authorization expires upon the withdrawal of the certificate. The holder of the authorization may file objections against the withdrawal of the certificate within 3 days of its delivery. The Ministry of Health decides on the objections. An appeal against the decision of the Ministry of Health on the objections is not possible.
§ 83d
(1) Authorization also expires for a reason other than under § 83c para. 5
a) by the expiry of the period for which it was granted, if no application for its extension was submitted by the holder of the authorization,
b) by the waiver of the certificate of authorization; the waiver is effective from the day it was delivered to the authorizing body,
c) in the case of natural persons, by the death or declaration of the holder of the authorization as deceased,
d) by the day of the dissolution of the legal person who is the holder of the authorization,
e) by the declaration of bankruptcy of the holder of the authorization, the rejection of a bankruptcy petition for the holder of the authorization for lack of assets, or the entry of the holder of the authorization into liquidation.
(2) The authorizing body in cases under paragraph 1 let. a) and under § 83c para. 5, the holder of the authorization, or their heir, the legal successor of the legal person, or its liquidator, in cases under paragraph 1 let. b) to e), are obliged to inform the Ministry of Health for the purposes under § 83c para. 3 of the date of the expiry of the authorization.
⁴⁷ᵃ⁾ § 21 para. 2 of the Commercial Code.".

At the end of the text of § 92 para. 3, a sentence is added, which reads: "A fine of up to CZK 1,000,000 may be imposed by this public health protection authority on a person who has acted without authorization as an authorizing body or a holder of authorization.".

After § 100, a new § 100a is inserted, which reads:
"§ 100a
If this Act or a special legal regulation governing the competence of a public health protection authority implies an obligation for a foreign person to submit documents confirming certain facts, it is understood as the submission of documents including their certified Czech translation, unless a special legal regulation provides otherwise. The authenticity of signatures and stamps on the original submitted documents must be verified.".

PART ELEVEN
EFFECTIVENESS

§ 137

This Act shall enter into force on 1 January 2002, with the exception of the provision of § 20 para. 1, which shall enter into force 5 years after the date of entry into force of this Act, and the provision of § 135, which shall enter into force on the day of its promulgation.

Final and Transitional Provisions introduced by Act No. 20/2004 Coll. Art. II

The fee declaration for determining the amount of advance payments of the fee for the abstracted quantity of groundwater for the year 2004 under § 88 para. 5 of the Water Act, as amended by this Act, shall be submitted by the abstractor to the Czech Environmental Inspectorate no later than 60 days from the date of entry into force of this Act.

The validity of permits for the abstraction of surface and groundwaters, with the exception of permits for the abstraction of groundwaters from sources intended for the individual supply of households with drinking water, and the validity of permits for the discharge of wastewater into surface or groundwaters, which became final by 31 December 2001, shall expire no later than 1 January 2008, unless they expire due to the expiry of the period for which they were granted, if this period is shorter. Authorizations (§ 8 para. 2 of the Water Act) from such permits shall continue to be considered as authorizations, and they may manage waters and exercise other rights and obligations to the extent of these permits even after 1 January 2008, provided they submitted an application for a permit for the management of waters replacing the previous permit no later than 1 January 2008, until the date the decision on such an application becomes final. If the period for which these decisions were granted expired before the effective date of this Act, their validity is extended until 31 December 2004. The provision of § 9 para. 4 of the Water Act is not affected by this point.

The records under § 21 para. 2 let. c) points 6, 7, 9 to 12 of the Water Act, as amended by this Act, shall be created no later than 22 December 2004.

The plan of the main river basins of the Czech Republic must be approved no later than 22 December 2006.

River basin district plans must be approved no later than 22 December 2009. For these river basin district plans, an analysis of the general and water management characteristics of the river basin districts, an assessment of the impacts of human activity on the status of surface and groundwaters, and an economic analysis of water use must be prepared under Art. I, point 30, regarding § 25 para. 2 let. a) of this Act, by 22 December 2004.

Municipalities whose currently built-up area is a source of pollution of a size greater than 2,000 population equivalents, or those that reach this size by 31 December 2010, are obliged to ensure the sewerage and treatment of their wastewater to the level set by a government regulation issued under § 38 para. 5 of the Water Act, as amended by this Act, no later than 31 December 2010.

The owners of waterworks under § 20 para. 1 of the Water Act, as amended by this Act, are obliged to submit to the relevant cadastral office the necessary documents for the registration of these structures and the marking of protection zones under § 20 para. 2 of the Water Act, as amended by this Act, in the real estate cadastre no later than 1 January 2011.

The assessments of fees for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters for the calendar year 2003 shall be issued by the regional authorities on the basis of the fee declarations for the year 2003. The regional authorities shall hand over to the Czech Environmental Inspectorate within 30 days of the entry into force of this Act the assessments of advance payments for the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters for the year 2004, including a list of the charged sources of pollution. The regional authorities shall hand over to the Czech Environmental Inspectorate within 30 days of the final force of the assessments of fees for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters for the year 2003.

Transitional Provisions introduced by Act No. 25/2008 Coll. § 14

Obligated subjects fulfilling reporting obligations defined in § 126 para. 6 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., on waters and on the amendment of certain acts (the Water Act), as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, who are also operators obliged to fulfill reporting obligations under Regulation (EC) No 166/2006 of the European Parliament and of the Council and under the Act on the integrated pollution register and the integrated system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment and on the amendment of certain acts, shall report the required data through the integrated system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment for the first time for the year 2009.

Obligated subjects fulfilling reporting obligations defined in § 126 para. 6 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., on waters and on the amendment of certain acts (the Water Act), as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, who are also operators of activities under Annex I to Regulation (EC) No 166/2006 of the European Parliament and of the Council and are not integrated into the system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment under point 1, shall report the required data through the integrated system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment for the first time for the year 2010. When reporting required data for the years 2008 and 2009, the previous legal regulations shall apply.

Obligated subjects fulfilling reporting obligations defined in § 126 para. 6 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., on waters and on the amendment of certain acts (the Water Act), as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, who are not integrated into the system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment under point 1 or 2, shall report the required data through the integrated system for fulfilling reporting obligations in the field of the environment for the first time for the year 2011. When reporting required data for the years 2008 to 2010, the previous legal regulations shall apply.

Transitional Provisions introduced by Act No. 181/2008 Coll. Art. II

The owners of waterworks specified in § 20 para. 1 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective until the date of entry into force of this Act, classified from the perspective of technical safety supervision under § 61 para. 2 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective until the date of entry into force of this Act, into categories I to III, are obliged to submit to the relevant cadastral office the necessary documents for the registration of these structures and the marking of protection zones under § 20 para. 2 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, in the real estate cadastre no later than 1 January 2011. The owners of other waterworks under § 20 para. 1 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, are obliged to fulfill this obligation by 1 January 2021.

Proceedings that were not finally concluded before the date of entry into force of this Act shall be concluded according to the previous legal regulations. If a decision that was issued in a proceeding under the previous legal regulations was annulled and returned for a new hearing, the procedure shall be according to the previous legal regulations.

For compensation for damage to agriculturally managed lands in the inundation areas of dry reservoirs serving for the protection of the territory of municipalities, regions, or the state, built before the date of entry into force of this Act, § 68 para. 2 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, shall apply mutatis mutandis.

The Minister of Finance is authorized to use the resources designated for the removal of flood damages incurred in 2006 and for new flood protection measures, which were transferred to state financial assets, also for the removal of flood damages incurred after 2006 on watercourses and waterworks. The total budgetary expenditures of the state budget are increased by this use, and the balances on the accounts of state financial assets are reduced.

Transitional Provisions introduced by Act No. 150/2010 Coll. Art. II

Permits for the abstraction of groundwater used for the production of bottled infant or spring water are considered permits for the abstraction of groundwater under Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, provided that the requirements under § 9 para. 4 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, are met; otherwise, they shall expire on the date of entry into force of this Act.

Protection zones established under previous legal regulations are considered protection zones established under § 30 para. 1 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act. In the event of a change or revocation of a previously established protection zone under previous legal regulations, the protection zone must be newly established according to the procedure under § 30 para. 1 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act.

Floodplains established under previous legal regulations are considered floodplains established under § 66 para. 7 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act. In the event of a change or revocation of a previously established floodplain under previous legal regulations, the floodplain must be newly established according to the procedure under § 66 para. 7 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act.

The assessment of flood risks and the definition of areas with significant flood risk must be carried out no later than 22 December 2011. Flood hazard maps and flood risk maps will be completed by 22 December 2013.

National river basin plans and flood risk management plans must be approved no later than 22 December 2015.

Water authorities are obliged, in their decision-making, issuance of opinions, and in the implementation of other measures under Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, to be guided by the approved plans of the relevant river basin districts until the approval of new plans under this Act in the relevant river basins.

The general plan of areas protected for surface water accumulation under § 28a para. 2 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as amended by Act No. 181/2008 Coll., is reviewed and updated within the framework of national river basin plans.

Proceedings that were not finally concluded before the date of entry into force of this Act shall be concluded according to the previous legal regulations.

The authorized water authorities under § 105 para. 2 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective until the date of entry into force of this Act, shall conclude initiated and not finally concluded proceedings.

Transitional Provision introduced by Act No. 151/2011 Coll. Art. IV

Bathing water profiles under § 34 para. 1 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, shall be created for the first time by 24 March 2011.

Transitional Provision introduced by Act No. 350/2012 Coll. Art. XVIII

Proceedings initiated before the date of entry into force of this Act shall be concluded according to the previous legal regulations.

Transitional Provision introduced by Act No. 501/2012 Coll. Art. V

Financial resources provided under § 6 para. 3 of Act No. 331/1993 Coll., on the state budget of the Czech Republic for the year 1994 and on the amendment and supplementation of certain acts, may be used to cover expenditures on measures in the public interest under § 102 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, and to support the construction and renewal of water management infrastructure.

Transitional Provision introduced by Act No. 275/2013 Coll. Art. IV

If a permit for the management of waters for the purpose of fish or waterfowl farming, or possibly other animals, specifies conditions for feeding or supplemental feeding of fish, or if these conditions are established by an exemption from the use of harmful substances, the decision in these parts need not be applied for the supplemental feeding of fish, and the procedure under § 39 para. 13 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, may be followed.

Transitional Provision introduced by Act No. 303/2013 Coll. Art. LV

If no agreement is reached between the landowner and the owner of the waterwork on compensation for the use of the land under § 59a of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, within 24 months from the date of entry into force of this Act, a court shall decide on the amount of compensation at the proposal of the landowner or the owner of the waterwork.

Transitional Provision introduced by Act No. 61/2014 Coll. Art. VI

Proceedings that were not finally concluded before the date of entry into force of this Act shall be concluded according to Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective before the date of entry into force of this Act.

Transitional Provision introduced by Act No. 225/2017 Coll. Art. XXXI

Administrative proceedings initiated before the date of entry into force of this Act shall be concluded according to the previous legal regulations.

Transitional Provisions introduced by Act No. 113/2018 Coll. Art. II

The obligation of the owner of a tank under § 38 para. 8 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, to submit documents on the removal of wastewater for the period of the last 2 calendar years applies to the period from the date of entry into force of this provision.

For fee obligations for the fee for the abstracted quantity of groundwater, as well as for the rights and obligations related thereto, that arose before the date of entry into force of this Act, Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective before the date of entry into force of this Act, shall apply.

For fee obligations for fees for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters, as well as for the rights and obligations related thereto, that arose before the date of entry into force of this Act, Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective before the date of entry into force of this Act, shall apply.

The provision of § 93 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective before the date of entry into force of this Act, shall not apply to advance payments of fees for the fee period of 2019.

For fee obligations for the fee for the permitted discharge of wastewater into groundwaters, as well as for the rights and obligations related thereto, that arose before the date of entry into force of this Act, Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective before the date of entry into force of this Act, shall apply.

The discharge of wastewater from the relief chamber of a unified sewer system that does not meet the technical requirements for its construction and operation as stipulated by the legal regulation implementing the Act on Water Supply and Sewerage Systems is exempt from the fee for the discharge of wastewater into surface waters until the fee period of 2022 inclusive.

Transitional Provisions introduced by Act No. 312/2019 Coll. Art. IV

Administrative proceedings that were not finally concluded before the date of entry into force of this Act shall be concluded by the water authority according to the previous legal regulations.

Procedures that are not administrative proceedings, initiated before the date of entry into force of this Act, shall be concluded by the water authority according to the previous legal regulations.

Transitional Provisions introduced by Act No. 544/2020 Coll. Art. II

The Ministry of Agriculture and the Ministry of the Environment shall prepare and publish a drought plan for the territory of the Czech Republic no later than 36 months from the date of entry into force of this Act.

The regional authority shall prepare and publish a drought plan for the territory of the region no later than 24 months from the date of entry into force of this Act.

The regional governor shall establish a regional drought commission no later than 3 months from the date of entry into force of this Act.

An authorized person who has a permit for the management of waters under § 8 para. 1 let. a) point 1 or § 8 para. 1 let. b) point 1 in a total quantity under § 10 para. 1, first sentence of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, is obliged to measure the quantity of water they abstract, for the first time in the year 2022, and to submit the results of this measurement by 31 January 2023.

The 6-month period specified in § 59 para. 1 let. k) of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective from the date of entry into force of this Act, applies to waterworks notified after the date of entry into force of this Act.

The validity of advance payment assessments for the abstracted quantity of groundwater issued by the Czech Environmental Inspectorate under § 88 para. 7 of Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective until 31 December 2018, shall expire on the date of entry into force of this Act.

Administrative proceedings that were initiated under Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective before the date of entry into force of this Act, and were not finally concluded before the date of entry into force of this Act, shall be concluded according to Act No. 254/2001 Coll., as effective before the date of entry into force of this Act.

Annex No. 1 to Act No. 254/2001 Coll.
Particularly Hazardous and Hazardous Harmful Substances

I. Particularly Hazardous Harmful Substances

Particularly hazardous harmful substances are substances belonging to the groups of substances listed below, with the exception of those that are biologically harmless or rapidly change into biologically harmless substances:

Organohalogen compounds and substances that can form such compounds in the aquatic environment,

Organophosphorus compounds,

Organotin compounds,

Substances or their decomposition products for which carcinogenic or mutagenic properties have been demonstrated, which may affect steroid production, the thyroid gland, reproduction, or other endocrine functions in or via the aquatic environment,

Mercury and its compounds,

Cadmium and its compounds,

Persistent mineral oils and persistent hydrocarbons of petroleum origin,

Persistent synthetic substances that can float, remain in suspension, or sink to the bottom and which can interfere with any use of water.

Individual particularly hazardous harmful substances are listed under the designation "particularly hazardous harmful substance" or "priority hazardous substance" in the government regulation issued under § 39 para. 3; other substances belonging to the listed groups but not designated in the government regulation as a particularly hazardous harmful substance or a priority hazardous substance are considered hazardous harmful substances.

II. Hazardous Harmful Substances

Hazardous harmful substances are substances belonging to the groups of substances listed below:

Compounds of metalloids and metals:

zinc

copper

nickel

chromium

lead

selenium

arsenic

antimony

molybdenum

titanium

tin

barium

beryllium

bor

uranium

vanadium

cobalt

thallium

tellurium

silver

Biocides and their derivatives not listed in the list of particularly hazardous harmful substances.

Substances that have a harmful effect on the taste or smell of products for human consumption originating from the aquatic environment, and compounds capable of increasing the content of these substances in water.

Toxic or persistent organic silicon compounds and substances that can increase the content of these compounds in water, except those that are biologically harmless or rapidly convert in water to harmless substances.

Elemental phosphorus and inorganic phosphorus compounds.

Non-persistent mineral oils and non-persistent hydrocarbons of petroleum origin.

Fluorides.

Substances that have an adverse effect on the oxygen balance, especially ammonium salts and nitrites.

Cyanides.

Sedimentable solid substances that have an adverse effect on the good status of surface waters.
